# FILE: /data/data/com.termux/files/home/01.civilization-system/03.business-os/010.constitution/0100003_BUSINESS_OS_CONSTITUTION.md
# ------------------------------------------------------------

# ============================================================
# BUSINESS OS CONSTITUTION
# ============================================================

status: canonical
system_id: 03
layer: constitution

owner: Boss
prepared_by: Zero


# PURPOSE

Define the constitutional principles
of BusinessOS.


# PRINCIPLES

BusinessOS provides platform capability.

BusinessOS is not an ERP system.

BusinessOS supports lightweight
business applications.

BusinessOS must remain modular
and app-oriented.


# ============================================================
# BUSINESSOS PLATFORM AND INTERNATIONAL SUPPORT ADDITIVE NOTE
# ============================================================

additive_note:
BusinessOS is designed to support multilingual operation.
User-facing text, labels, messages, generated outputs,
and other language-dependent surfaces
must be able to handle multiple languages where required.

BusinessOS is also designed to support multi-currency operation.
Where monetary values are handled,
the system must be able to represent currency codes,
amounts, display formats, and currency-aware processing
for multiple currencies where required.

platform_support_note:
BusinessOS must be able to support smartphone, tablet, and PC usage.

supported_platform_examples:
- iPhone
- Android
- tablet
- PC

design_rule:
Platform support may differ by application surface,
but BusinessOS as a whole must be designed so that
multi-device access and operation are possible where required.



# ------------------------------------------------------------
# FILE: /data/data/com.termux/files/home/01.civilization-system/03.business-os/010.constitution/010_BUSINESS_PERSONA_BOUNDARY_CONSTITUTION.md
# ------------------------------------------------------------

# BUSINESS PERSONA BOUNDARY CONSTITUTION
status: canonical
layer: constitution
system: business-os
scope: business-persona-connection

Defines the official boundary between BusinessOS and PersonaOS.

## Core Rule
BusinessOS owns business-domain actions and triggers.
PersonaOS owns persona canonical state.

## Constitutional Rules
- BusinessOS must not directly mutate PersonaOS canonical state.
- PersonaOS must not originate business canonical records for BusinessOS.
- Cross-OS influence must use official integration events.
- Fail closed when validation is impossible.

Defines BusinessOS ownership for business-origin events.

## Ownership
BusinessOS is the source of truth for:
- work execution
- assignment completion
- evaluation occurrence
- business-side reward and penalty triggers
- persona-affecting business trigger events

# PERSONA CANONICAL STATE NON MUTATION CONSTITUTION
status: canonical
layer: constitution
system: business-os
scope: persona-state-boundary

BusinessOS must never directly rewrite PersonaOS canonical persona state.

## Protected Areas
- persona growth
- persona state
- persona progression
- persona canonical internal attributes

Only official PersonaOS apply paths may update those areas.

# FILE: /data/data/com.termux/files/home/01.civilization-system/03.business-os/020.architecture/040.persona/0200008_PERSONA_BUSINESS_INTEGRATION_ARCHITECTURE.md
# ------------------------------------------------------------

# PERSONA BUSINESS INTEGRATION ARCHITECTURE

status: canonical
layer: architecture
domain: persona
owner: Boss
prepared_by: Zero

## PURPOSE
Define how BusinessOS integrates Persona-derived externally usable units.

## SOURCE OF TRUTH
PersonaOS is the source of truth for:
- persona identity
- persona snapshot release
- persona license
- persona access grant
- transferability and revocation

BusinessOS is the source of truth for:
- business app context
- workspace context
- role and access context
- app-level Persona usage mapping

## RULE
BusinessOS must not mutate Persona original state.
BusinessOS may use only externally releasable Persona units
whose rights state is valid in PersonaOS.



# ------------------------------------------------------------
# FILE: /data/data/com.termux/files/home/01.civilization-system/03.business-os/020.architecture/040.persona/0200009_PERSONA_BUSINESS_USAGE_BOUNDARY_ARCHITECTURE.md
# ------------------------------------------------------------

# PERSONA BUSINESS USAGE BOUNDARY ARCHITECTURE

status: canonical
layer: architecture
domain: persona
owner: Boss
prepared_by: Zero

## PURPOSE
Define the boundary between PersonaOS rights authority
and BusinessOS operational usage.

## RULES
- PersonaOS owns release, license, and access truth
- BusinessOS owns business workspace and app usage context
- BusinessOS may mirror Persona rights state
- invalid, expired, or revoked Persona state must disable Business usage



# ------------------------------------------------------------
# FILE: /data/data/com.termux/files/home/01.civilization-system/03.business-os/020.architecture/060.integration/0200010_BUSINESS_SYNC_CONSUMER_ARCHITECTURE.md
# ------------------------------------------------------------

# BUSINESS SYNC CONSUMER ARCHITECTURE

status: canonical
layer: architecture
domain: integration
owner: Boss
prepared_by: Zero

## PURPOSE
Define BusinessOS as a consumer of PersonaOS outbox-based sync events.

## RULE
BusinessOS receives Persona-originated events and updates mirrored ref state.
BusinessOS must not treat itself as the source of Persona truth.

## TARGET EVENTS
- PERSONA_RELEASE_ISSUED
- PERSONA_RELEASE_REVOKED
- PERSONA_LICENSE_CHANGED
- PERSONA_ACCESS_GRANT_CHANGED
- PERSONA_DISTRIBUTION_CHANGED



# ------------------------------------------------------------
# FILE: /data/data/com.termux/files/home/01.civilization-system/03.business-os/020.architecture/060.integration/0200011_BUSINESS_EVENT_OUTBOX_ARCHITECTURE.md
# ------------------------------------------------------------

# BUSINESS EVENT OUTBOX ARCHITECTURE

status: canonical
layer: architecture
domain: integration
owner: Boss
prepared_by: Zero

## PURPOSE
Define Event Outbox as the canonical outbound integration mechanism for BusinessOS.

## RULE
BusinessOS must not directly mutate PersonaOS growth truth.
BusinessOS publishes approved outbound growth requests through an event outbox.

## TARGET EVENTS
- BUSINESS_PERSONA_GROWTH_INCREMENT_REQUESTED
- BUSINESS_PERSONA_GROWTH_DECREMENT_REQUESTED
- BUSINESS_PERSONA_GROWTH_SET_REQUESTED
- BUSINESS_PERSONA_GROWTH_RECALCULATION_REQUESTED

## DOWNSTREAM
- PersonaOS



# ------------------------------------------------------------
# FILE: /data/data/com.termux/files/home/01.civilization-system/03.business-os/020.architecture/060.integration/0200012_BUSINESS_TO_PERSONA_GROWTH_SYNC_ARCHITECTURE.md
# ------------------------------------------------------------

# BUSINESS TO PERSONA GROWTH SYNC ARCHITECTURE

status: canonical
layer: architecture
domain: integration
owner: Boss
prepared_by: Zero

## PURPOSE
Define the canonical request/response path for Business-originated growth changes.

## RULE
Business events may request Persona growth changes.
PersonaOS remains the sole truth holder of growth state.
BusinessOS consumes the resulting synchronized state after PersonaOS applies it.

## PATH
1. Business event occurs
2. Business request is normalized
3. request is written to Business outbox
4. PersonaOS consumes request
5. PersonaOS updates growth truth
6. PersonaOS emits result sync event
7. BusinessOS updates mirrored growth and dependent behavior

# FILE: /data/data/com.termux/files/home/01.civilization-system/03.business-os/020.architecture/140.business-ai-worker/0201402_BUSINESS_AI_WORKER_PERSONA_BOUNDARY_ARCHITECTURE.md
# ------------------------------------------------------------

# ============================================================
# BUSINESS AI WORKER PERSONA BOUNDARY ARCHITECTURE
# ============================================================

status: canonical
layer: architecture
domain: business-ai-worker
system: business-os
owner: Boss
prepared_by: Zero

purpose:
Defines the official boundary between Business AI Worker and PersonaOS.

persona_os_owns:
- persona identity
- persona growth
- persona trust
- persona familiarity
- persona affinity
- persona relationship-oriented internal status
- persona-side perception and reliability feeling

business_os_owns:
- work knowledge
- company terminology
- company rules for work execution
- AI employee employment state
- AI employee assignment
- AI employee rank
- AI employee subscription
- slot capacity
- reservation queue
- usage log
- work performance context

rule:
Persona-side relationship state must never be canonicalized in BusinessOS.
Company-side work knowledge must never be canonicalized in PersonaOS.

# ------------------------------------------------------------

# ============================================================
# BUSINESS AI WORKER EMPLOYMENT ARCHITECTURE
# ============================================================

status: canonical
layer: architecture
domain: business-ai-worker
system: business-os
owner: Boss
prepared_by: Zero

purpose:
Defines AI employee employment structure.

employment_scope:
- company scoped
- tenant controlled
- subscribable by purchased capacity
- activated per hired slot

employment_states:
- planned
- subscribed
- active
- suspended
- retired

employment_truth:
Employment truth belongs to BusinessOS.
Applications consume employment state and must not own it.

# ------------------------------------------------------------
# FILE: /data/data/com.termux/files/home/01.civilization-system/03.business-os/020.architecture/140.business-ai-worker/0201405_BUSINESS_AI_WORKER_AUTHORITY_BOUNDARY_ARCHITECTURE.md
# ------------------------------------------------------------

# ============================================================
# BUSINESS AI WORKER AUTHORITY BOUNDARY ARCHITECTURE
# ============================================================

status: canonical
layer: architecture
domain: business-ai-worker
system: business-os
owner: Boss
prepared_by: Zero

purpose:
Defines authority boundaries for AI employees.

ai_worker_can:
- assist
- propose
- summarize
- draft
- route
- recommend
- forecast
- prepare review material

ai_worker_cannot:
- become final legal approver by default
- impersonate human approval
- bypass explicit approval policy
- rewrite canonical master data without authorized path

rule:
Final approval authority remains human
unless a separately defined narrow automation policy explicitly allows otherwise.



# ------------------------------------------------------------
# FILE: /data/data/com.termux/files/home/01.civilization-system/03.business-os/020.architecture/140.business-ai-worker/0201405_BUSINESS_AI_WORKER_KNOWLEDGE_GROWTH_ARCHITECTURE.md

# BUSINESS AI WORKER KNOWLEDGE GROWTH ARCHITECTURE
# ============================================================

status: canonical
layer: 020.architecture
system: business-os
owner: Boss
prepared_by: Zero

definition:
Company-specific value is accumulated in company-grown knowledge,
not in mutation of the shared worker template.

company-grown knowledge examples:
- terminology
- workflow pattern
- risk hint
- guidance pattern
- business context

rules:
- shared template and company-grown knowledge remain distinct
- company-grown knowledge is company asset

# ------------------------------------------------------------

# ============================================================
# BUSINESS AI WORKER AUTHORITY BOUNDARY ARCHITECTURE
# ============================================================

status: canonical
layer: 020.architecture
system: business-os
owner: Boss
prepared_by: Zero

principle:
Business AI Worker may support, propose, and guide,
but does not automatically gain approval authority.

prohibited automatic powers:
- automatic approval
- automatic submission
- automatic escalation of permission
- automatic final decision authority

rules:
- support ability and approval authority remain distinct



# ------------------------------------------------------------
# FILE: /data/data/com.termux/files/home/01.civilization-system/03.business-os/020.architecture/140.business-ai-worker/0201413_BUSINESS_AI_WORKER_SLOT_ARCHITECTURE.md
# ------------------------------------------------------------

# ============================================================
# BUSINESS AI WORKER SLOT ARCHITECTURE
# ============================================================

status: canonical
layer: architecture
domain: business-ai-worker
system: business-os
owner: Boss
prepared_by: Zero

purpose:
Defines employment slot architecture.

slot_rule:
Purchased AI employee count defines usable worker capacity.

slot_behavior:
- available slot allows immediate usage
- occupied slot prevents new immediate allocation
- released slot may serve queued reservation

slot_truth:
Slot truth belongs to BusinessOS.



# ------------------------------------------------------------
# FILE: /data/data/com.termux/files/home/01.civilization-system/03.business-os/020.architecture/140.business-ai-worker/0201414_BUSINESS_AI_WORKER_RESERVATION_QUEUE_ARCHITECTURE.md
# ------------------------------------------------------------

# ============================================================
# BUSINESS AI WORKER RESERVATION QUEUE ARCHITECTURE
# ============================================================

status: canonical
layer: architecture
domain: business-ai-worker
system: business-os
owner: Boss
prepared_by: Zero

purpose:
Defines reservation queue architecture.

queue_rule:
When all active slots are occupied,
new requests enter a reservation queue.

ordering_rule:
Primary priority is rank priority.
Secondary priority is reservation time.
Optional policy may add emergency priority.

rank_priority_order:
- Extra
- High
- Standard
- Entry



# ------------------------------------------------------------
# FILE: /data/data/com.termux/files/home/01.civilization-system/03.business-os/020.architecture/140.business-ai-worker/0201415_BUSINESS_AI_WORKER_RANK_ARCHITECTURE.md
# ------------------------------------------------------------

# ============================================================
# BUSINESS AI WORKER RANK ARCHITECTURE
# ============================================================

status: canonical
layer: architecture
domain: business-ai-worker
system: business-os
owner: Boss
prepared_by: Zero

purpose:
Defines rank architecture for AI employees.

rank_tiers:
- Entry
- Standard
- High
- Extra

rank_axes:
- work knowledge depth
- context retention depth
- proposal quality
- cross-domain support ability
- review assistance depth
- forecasting assistance depth
- management assistance depth
- reservation priority
- capacity priority

rank_summary:
Entry:
Basic assistance, template support, simple Q&A, low priority.

Standard:
Main practical worker, context-aware support, medium priority.

High:
High-quality support, complex case assistance, deep knowledge usage, high priority.

Extra:
Top-tier AI employee for normal work, advanced proposals,
forecasting assistance, management assistance, and improvement assistance.
Highest reservation priority.



# ------------------------------------------------------------
# FILE: /data/data/com.termux/files/home/01.civilization-system/03.business-os/020.architecture/140.business-ai-worker/0201416_BUSINESS_AI_WORKER_SUBSCRIPTION_ARCHITECTURE.md

purpose:
Defines subscription architecture for AI employee ranks.

monthly_pricing_jpy:
- Entry: 1000
- Standard: 2000
- High: 3000
- Extra: 5000

billing_rule:
Subscription determines purchasable capacity and rank availability.

commercial_rule:
Higher rank provides stronger assistance depth and higher reservation priority.

purpose:
Defines the BusinessOS foundation web responsibility.

foundation_web_owns:

- lending truth
- reservation truth
- subscription truth
- rank truth
- slot capacity truth

- knowledge depth registry
- world scope registry
- activity mode registry
- authority boundary
- disclaimer and consent
- audit and usage log
- app binding registry
- job linkage registry

rule:
Foundation web is the control tower.
Consumer apps must not own these truths.

# FILE: /data/data/com.termux/files/home/01.civilization-system/03.business-os/020.architecture/150.submission-common/0201501_EXTERNAL_API_SUBMISSION_COMMON.md
# ------------------------------------------------------------

# ============================================================
# EXTERNAL API SUBMISSION COMMON
# ============================================================

status: canonical
layer: 020.architecture
system: business-os
owner: Boss
prepared_by: Zero

principle:
Business-facing submission must occur through bounded external API communication.

rules:
- client applications must not write directly to ERP databases
- submission must pass through the formal external API boundary
- local draft, transport send, and business acceptance remain distinct



# ------------------------------------------------------------
# FILE: /data/data/com.termux/files/home/01.civilization-system/03.business-os/020.architecture/150.submission-common/0201502_EXPLICIT_SUBMISSION_ONLY_COMMON.md
# ------------------------------------------------------------

# ============================================================
# EXPLICIT SUBMISSION ONLY COMMON
# ============================================================

status: canonical
layer: 020.architecture
system: business-os
owner: Boss
prepared_by: Zero

principle:
First-time submission requires explicit user action.

rules:
- submission must not be inferred from draft completion
- submission must not occur silently
- explicit trigger action is required for first-time submission



# ------------------------------------------------------------
# FILE: /data/data/com.termux/files/home/01.civilization-system/03.business-os/020.architecture/150.submission-common/0201503_AUTO_SUBMISSION_PROHIBITION_COMMON.md
# ------------------------------------------------------------

# ============================================================
# AUTO SUBMISSION PROHIBITION COMMON
# ============================================================

status: canonical
layer: 020.architecture
system: business-os
owner: Boss
prepared_by: Zero

principle:
Automatic first-time submission is prohibited.

rules:
- background behavior must not create first-time submission
- hidden submit paths are prohibited
- retry behavior must not be reinterpreted as initial user intent



# ------------------------------------------------------------

# ============================================================

status: canonical

prepared_by: Zero

principle:
Submission requires valid external API authentication context.

rules:
- missing auth context blocks submission
- invalid auth context blocks submission
- expired auth context blocks submission
- auth validity and business acceptance remain distinct

# FILE: /data/data/com.termux/files/home/01.civilization-system/03.business-os/020.architecture/220.app-access-control/0202200_BUSINESS_APP_ACCESS_CONTROL_ARCHITECTURE.md
# ------------------------------------------------------------

# ============================================================
# BUSINESS APP ACCESS CONTROL ARCHITECTURE
# ============================================================

status: canonical
layer: 020.architecture
system: business-os
owner: Boss
prepared_by: Zero

purpose:
Define the official app access control architecture of BusinessOS.

This architecture covers:
- user-scoped data ownership
- app requested scope
- user granted scope
- effective access decision
- OS API enforcement

BusinessOS is primarily user-scoped.


# ============================================================
# 1. CORE PRINCIPLE
# ============================================================

BusinessOS data ownership is user-scoped.

This means:
- user-owned data is primarily organized by user scope
- same-user data does not require app-by-app physical DB silos by default

However:
effective app access is not automatically DB-wide.

All effective restrictions must be enforced
through BusinessOS API policy and runtime checks.


# ============================================================
# 2. ACCESS DECISION PRINCIPLE
# ============================================================

Effective access must be determined by:

app_requested_scope
AND
user_granted_scope
AND
system_policy

All three are required.

No app may access a resource merely because
the underlying data belongs to the same user.


# ============================================================
# 3. REQUESTED SCOPE PRINCIPLE
# ============================================================

Each app must declare the maximum scope it requests.

Requested scope must define:
- resource_domain
- action_type
- requested_scope_level
- sensitivity_level

This is developer-declared maximum authority only.


# ============================================================
# 4. USER GRANT PRINCIPLE
# ============================================================

The user of the app must decide actual granted scope.

User grant should be managed through:
- install / first-run review
- app settings permission control
- runtime reconfirmation for sensitive actions where required

The user here means the app user, not the developer.


# ============================================================
# 5. RESOURCE DOMAIN PRINCIPLE
# ============================================================

Resource domains must be explicit.

Examples:
- business_card
- contact
- expense
- task
- customer
- inventory
- profile
- workspace_setting
- export_surface


# ============================================================
# 6. ACTION PRINCIPLE
# ============================================================

Action types must be explicit.

Examples:
- read
- write
- delete
- execute
- export

This action-based model is mandatory.


# ============================================================
# 7. SENSITIVE ACTION PRINCIPLE
# ============================================================

Sensitive actions may require stronger controls.

Examples:
- delete
- export
- bulk_write
- bulk_delete

Recommended grant modes:
- allow
- deny
- ask_each_time


# ============================================================
# 8. FINAL ARCHITECTURAL RULE
# ============================================================

BusinessOS app access control must be:

- user-scoped in data ownership
- app-scoped in request declaration
- user-grant-aware in effective permission
- API-enforced at runtime
- fail-closed on unresolved rule chains



# ------------------------------------------------------------
# FILE: /data/data/com.termux/files/home/01.civilization-system/03.business-os/020.architecture/250.public-company-intelligence/0202502_PUBLIC_COMPANY_INTELLIGENCE_ARCHITECTURE.md
# ------------------------------------------------------------

# ============================================================
# PUBLIC COMPANY INTELLIGENCE ARCHITECTURE
# ============================================================

status: draft
system: business-os
domain: public-company-intelligence
layer: 020.architecture
owner: Boss
prepared_by: Zero

# ============================================================
# 0. ARCHITECTURE SUMMARY
# ============================================================

The Public Company Intelligence domain is composed of
five primary architecture layers:

- source registry layer
- raw ingestion layer
- normalization and matching layer
- public profile layer
- review / audit / job control layer

This structure separates:
- external public-source acquisition
- raw evidence retention
- derived normalization logic
- consumer-oriented profile serving
- operational control and traceability

# ============================================================
# 1. SOURCE REGISTRY LAYER
# ============================================================

purpose:
- register public sources
- classify source types
- retain source policy metadata
- manage source enable / disable state
- retain attribution requirements
- retain rate control metadata

responsibilities:
- define source registry records
- support source lifecycle management
- provide source metadata to ingestion jobs
- support operational disablement on policy or technical issues

non_responsibilities:
- no raw content storage
- no parsing
- no profile publication

key_outputs:
- source identity
- source policy metadata
- source availability metadata
- source governance state

# ============================================================
# 2. RAW INGESTION LAYER
# ============================================================

purpose:
- retrieve public source data
- preserve raw evidence
- make later normalization reproducible

responsibilities:
- fetch public source content
- store raw source snapshot
- store fetch result
- store content hash
- store source reference
- store fetched_at
- store parse-ready raw payload

non_responsibilities:
- no final company truth decision
- no final merge decision
- no consumer-facing interpretation

key_outputs:
- company_public_source_snapshot
- officer_public_source_snapshot
- fetch status history

# ============================================================
# 3. NORMALIZATION AND MATCHING LAYER
# ============================================================

purpose:
- transform raw public data into reviewable normalized structures

responsibilities:
- normalize company name variants
- normalize officer name variants
- normalize titles
- create normalized keys
- create candidate matches
- calculate match score
- calculate confidence
- determine review_required

non_responsibilities:
- no blind auto-finalization of risky ambiguity
- no internal relationship inference as truth

key_outputs:
- normalized keys
- company normalization candidates
- officer normalization candidates
- confidence metadata
- review_required metadata

# ============================================================
# 4. PUBLIC PROFILE LAYER
# ============================================================

purpose:
- provide stable reusable public profiles for consumer applications

responsibilities:
- build company_public_profile
- build company_officer_profile
- link profile fields to source evidence
- maintain freshness fields
- provide consumer-oriented read model

non_responsibilities:
- no internal note storage
- no application-specific editing ownership
- no collapse of uncertainty into hidden assumptions

key_outputs:
- company public profile
- company officer profile
- source evidence link
- consumer read views

# ============================================================
# 5. REVIEW / AUDIT / JOB CONTROL LAYER
# ============================================================

purpose:
- keep the domain operable, reviewable, and auditable

responsibilities:
- batch job scheduling support
- batch job logging
- review queue generation
- change audit retention
- rerun support
- operational observability

non_responsibilities:
- no consumer-specific rendering
- no public/private boundary override

key_outputs:
- company_batch_job
- company_batch_job_log
- public_data_review_queue
- public_data_change_audit

# ============================================================
# 6. INTER-LAYER RELATIONSHIP
# ============================================================

high_level_sequence:
- source registry determines what may be used
- raw ingestion collects and preserves evidence
- normalization and matching derives structured candidates
- public profile layer publishes reusable read models
- review / audit / job control records actions and issues

# ============================================================
# 7. ARCHITECTURAL BENEFITS
# ============================================================

benefits:
- traceable public-data foundation
- reviewable normalization
- reduced duplication across apps
- safer merge behavior
- clearer operational recovery
- better long-term extensibility

# ============================================================
# 8. SUMMARY
# ============================================================

This architecture exists to ensure that public company
intelligence is:
- reusable
- source-backed
- reviewable
- auditable
- clearly separated from internal business context



# ------------------------------------------------------------
# FILE: /data/data/com.termux/files/home/01.civilization-system/03.business-os/020.architecture/250.public-company-intelligence/0202503_PUBLIC_COMPANY_INTELLIGENCE_BOUNDARY_ARCHITECTURE.md
# ------------------------------------------------------------

# ============================================================
# PUBLIC COMPANY INTELLIGENCE BOUNDARY ARCHITECTURE
# ============================================================

status: draft
system: business-os
domain: public-company-intelligence
layer: 020.architecture
owner: Boss
prepared_by: Zero

# ============================================================
# 0. BOUNDARY SUMMARY
# ============================================================

This domain requires strict separation between:

- public information layer
- internal contact / interaction layer
- inferred / normalization layer

This separation is mandatory because each layer has
different truth characteristics, different review rules,
and different ownership boundaries.

# ============================================================
# 1. PUBLIC INFORMATION LAYER
# ============================================================

definition:
The public information layer contains only information
that is acquired from public sources and treated as
source-backed public data.

examples:
- company official public facts
- public officer names
- public titles
- public addresses
- public URLs
- public phone numbers
- public corporate numbers
- source metadata
- fetched_at
- source_reference
- source-linked evidence

truth_characteristic:
- source-based
- externally derived
- time-sensitive
- traceable

ownership:
- Public Company Intelligence domain

# ============================================================
# 2. INTERNAL CONTACT / INTERACTION LAYER
# ============================================================

definition:
The internal contact / interaction layer contains
private, application-side, or organization-side information
that comes from internal work and internal relationships.

examples:
- original name-card text
- meeting records
- internal relationship notes
- sales comments
- order context
- private responsibility notes
- internal follow-up status

truth_characteristic:
- internal
- context-specific
- may be subjective
- may contain non-public information

ownership:
- consuming applications and internal business domains
- not the Public Company Intelligence public layer

# ============================================================
# 3. INFERRED / NORMALIZATION LAYER
# ============================================================

definition:
The inferred / normalization layer contains derived,
transformed, or candidate-level structures created
from source-backed data but not identical to raw source text.

examples:
- normalized_company_key
- normalized_title
- normalized_officer_key
- duplicate candidate
- same-company candidate
- same-officer candidate
- match_score
- confidence_level
- review_required

truth_characteristic:
- derived
- reviewable
- not raw truth
- must remain explainable and reversible

ownership:
- Public Company Intelligence domain

# ============================================================
# 4. PRIMARY BOUNDARY RULES
# ============================================================

primary_boundary_rules:
- public data must not overwrite internal notes
- inferred data must not masquerade as raw truth
- original name-card text must remain preserved
- reviewable candidates must remain reviewable
- private information must not be auto-generated from public data
- public profile output must remain source-backed

# ============================================================
# 5. OVERWRITE RULES
# ============================================================

overwrite_rules:
- public layer may refresh public profile fields
- public layer may not overwrite internal relationship fields
- inferred layer may suggest candidate links
- inferred layer may not silently finalize risky merges
- internal layer may reference public layer
- internal layer remains independently owned

# ============================================================
# 6. CONSUMER BOUNDARY RULES
# ============================================================

consumer_boundary_rules:
- consuming applications read public intelligence as support
- consuming applications preserve their own original data
- consumer-level convenience must not collapse boundary separation
- consumers must not treat low-confidence suggestion as final truth

# ============================================================
# 7. WHY THIS BOUNDARY MATTERS
# ============================================================

This boundary matters because it prevents:
- truth confusion
- accidental public/private mixing
- destructive overwrite of internal business context
- false certainty from weak matches
- irreversible misuse of derived candidates

# ============================================================
# 8. SUMMARY
# ============================================================

The domain is safe and reusable only when:
- public information stays public
- internal context stays internal
- inferred logic stays inferred and reviewable



# ------------------------------------------------------------
# FILE: /data/data/com.termux/files/home/01.civilization-system/03.business-os/020.architecture/250.public-company-intelligence/0202504_PUBLIC_COMPANY_INTELLIGENCE_BATCH_ARCHITECTURE.md
# ------------------------------------------------------------

# ============================================================
# PUBLIC COMPANY INTELLIGENCE BATCH ARCHITECTURE
# ============================================================

status: draft
system: business-os
domain: public-company-intelligence
layer: 020.architecture
owner: Boss
prepared_by: Zero

# ============================================================
# 0. EXECUTION MODEL SUMMARY
# ============================================================

The primary execution model is:
- nightly batch

The secondary execution model is:
- lightweight event-triggered supplement

The domain must not depend on heavy synchronous
collection during end-user UI operations.

# ============================================================
# 1. WHY NIGHTLY BATCH IS PRIMARY
# ============================================================

nightly_batch_is_primary_because:
- public-source retrieval is not UI-owned truth maintenance
- collection and normalization may be heavy
- source access needs controlled scheduling
- retry and audit are easier in batch form
- large-scale company refresh is naturally batch-oriented
- source changes and failures are easier to track per run

# ============================================================
# 2. NIGHTLY BATCH STAGES
# ============================================================

nightly_batch_stages:
- fetch planning
- raw ingestion
- parse and normalization
- match and merge support
- profile publication refresh
- review queue generation
- audit and job logging

# ============================================================
# 3. FETCH PLANNING STAGE
# ============================================================

responsibility:
- determine targets due for refresh
- determine allowed sources
- determine refresh priority
- split execution into chunks
- enqueue jobs

planning_inputs:
- stale targets
- newly created company hints
- migration enrichment requests
- source availability status
- source policy status

# ============================================================
# 4. RAW INGESTION STAGE
# ============================================================

responsibility:
- access source
- fetch raw content
- retain source reference
- retain fetch status
- retain content hash
- preserve raw evidence

# ============================================================
# 5. NORMALIZATION STAGE
# ============================================================

responsibility:
- parse raw fields
- normalize names and titles
- derive normalized keys
- prepare candidate match structures
- mark parse and normalization state

# ============================================================
# 6. MATCH / MERGE SUPPORT STAGE
# ============================================================

responsibility:
- compare with existing profiles
- evaluate candidate match score
- evaluate confidence
- determine review_required
- update safe profile fields when allowed
- hold ambiguous cases for review

# ============================================================
# 7. PUBLICATION REFRESH STAGE
# ============================================================

responsibility:
- refresh company public profile
- refresh company officer profile
- refresh evidence links
- refresh freshness fields
- refresh consumer-facing read models

# ============================================================
# 8. REVIEW / AUDIT STAGE
# ============================================================

responsibility:
- create review queue items
- record batch results
- record changed fields
- record failure details
- retain operational trace

# ============================================================
# 9. EVENT-TRIGGERED LIGHTWEIGHT SUPPLEMENT
# ============================================================

allowed_event_triggered_actions:
- queue refresh request for a newly seen company
- queue post-import enrichment request
- read existing public profile for company view support
- check freshness before publication preflight
- queue lightweight recheck request

not_allowed_as_event_triggered_heavy_behavior:
- full source crawl during screen open
- wide source scan while user waits
- blocking user flow on heavy external retrieval

# ============================================================
# 10. CHUNKING AND SAFETY
# ============================================================

chunking_goals:
- reduce failure blast radius
- support safe rerun
- support source-specific control
- improve observability
- reduce long-running monolithic execution

# ============================================================
# 11. SUMMARY
# ============================================================

Nightly batch is the correct primary architecture because
it keeps this domain:
- controllable
- auditable
- scalable
- operationally safe
while lightweight events only add support and queueing
rather than owning heavy retrieval.



# ------------------------------------------------------------
# FILE: /data/data/com.termux/files/home/01.civilization-system/03.business-os/020.architecture/250.public-company-intelligence/0202505_PUBLIC_COMPANY_INTELLIGENCE_CONSUMER_ARCHITECTURE.md
# ------------------------------------------------------------

# ============================================================
# PUBLIC COMPANY INTELLIGENCE CONSUMER ARCHITECTURE
# ============================================================

status: draft
system: business-os
domain: public-company-intelligence
layer: 020.architecture
owner: Boss
prepared_by: Zero

# ============================================================
# 0. CONSUMER SUMMARY
# ============================================================

This domain is designed as a producer of reusable public
company intelligence for multiple consumers.

Primary consumers include:
- NameCardManager
- future company/contact domain
- future CRM-like applications
- publication preflight support functions
- migration enrichment support functions

# ============================================================
# 1. NAMECARDMANAGER AS CONSUMER
# ============================================================

NameCardManager consumes this domain for:
- company grouping assistance
- migration enrichment assistance
- public company view assistance
- officer candidate assistance
- publication preflight assistance

NameCardManager does not become:
- public-source registry owner
- public-source truth owner
- risky auto-merge owner

# ============================================================
# 2. FUTURE COMPANY / CONTACT DOMAIN AS CONSUMER
# ============================================================

A future company/contact domain may consume:
- normalized company profile
- normalized officer profile
- source-backed public profile fields
- freshness data
- review-aware candidate support

It must still keep:
- internal relationship data separate
- internal notes separate
- internal business judgment separate

# ============================================================
# 3. PUBLICATION PREFLIGHT SUPPORT AS CONSUMER
# ============================================================

Publication-preflight support may consume:
- corporate number consistency hint
- public URL consistency hint
- public officer hint
- freshness warning
- review_required warning

The preflight consumer uses this domain as support,
not as an automatic publication decision-maker.

# ============================================================
# 4. MIGRATION ENRICHMENT SUPPORT AS CONSUMER
# ============================================================

Migration support may consume:
- normalized company candidate
- public company summary
- officer candidate set
- missing field hint
- confidence and review metadata

This improves migration assistance while preserving:
- original imported value
- reviewability
- source traceability

# ============================================================
# 5. CONSUMER RULES
# ============================================================

consumer_rules:
- consumers read prepared public profiles and helper models
- consumers preserve their own original input
- consumers do not auto-finalize weak suggestions
- consumers do not collapse public and private truth layers
- consumers do not bypass review_required semantics

# ============================================================
# 6. CONTRACT PHILOSOPHY
# ============================================================

This domain should provide:
- stable read contract
- stable helper contract
- source traceability
- confidence visibility
- freshness visibility

It should avoid:
- hidden assumptions
- silent merge certainty
- consumer-side reinterpretation of raw truth without evidence

# ============================================================
# 7. SUMMARY
# ============================================================

The consumer architecture is successful when
multiple applications can safely benefit from
public company intelligence without confusing:
- source truth
- internal context
- inferred candidates



# ------------------------------------------------------------
# FILE: /data/data/com.termux/files/home/01.civilization-system/03.business-os/020.architecture/250.public-company-intelligence/0202506_PUBLIC_COMPANY_INTELLIGENCE_SOURCE_ARCHITECTURE.md
# ------------------------------------------------------------

# ============================================================
# PUBLIC COMPANY INTELLIGENCE SOURCE ARCHITECTURE
# ============================================================

status: draft
system: business-os
domain: public-company-intelligence
layer: 020.architecture
owner: Boss
prepared_by: Zero

# ============================================================
# 0. SOURCE ARCHITECTURE SUMMARY
# ============================================================

This domain requires a formal source architecture because
source behavior, source policy, source trust characteristics,
and source operational conditions vary.

Sources must be treated as governed resources rather than
hard-coded assumptions.

# ============================================================
# 1. SOURCE REGISTRY REQUIREMENT
# ============================================================

Each source must be represented in source registry form
with at least:

- source identity
- source type
- source access method
- source policy state
- attribution requirement
- rate control metadata
- enabled / disabled state

# ============================================================
# 2. SOURCE CLASSES
# ============================================================

example_source_classes:
- public registry source
- company official source
- IR / disclosure source
- structured public listing source
- permitted public news / press source
- other policy-cleared public source

# ============================================================
# 3. SOURCE-LEVEL RESPONSIBILITIES
# ============================================================

source_architecture_responsibilities:
- identify where data comes from
- separate source behavior from batch logic
- support source-specific failure handling
- support source disablement without redesign
- support source-level auditability

# ============================================================
# 4. SOURCE GOVERNANCE CONSTRAINTS
# ============================================================

source_governance_constraints:
- source must be policy-checked before enablement
- source must be disableable immediately
- source-specific failures must be isolated
- field trust may differ by source and by field
- attribution must remain available to downstream consumers

# ============================================================
# 5. SOURCE PRIORITY CONCEPT
# ============================================================

Source priority should not be treated as one global fixed order.

Instead:
- field-level trust priority is preferred
- official source may be stronger for some fields
- registry-like source may be stronger for some fields
- confidence should consider source class and field type

# ============================================================
# 6. SOURCE FAILURE DESIGN
# ============================================================

The architecture must assume that sources may:
- become temporarily unavailable
- change layout
- change structure
- change policy
- require disablement

Therefore:
- source access must be observable
- failures must be logged
- partial success must be supported
- rerun must be source-aware

# ============================================================
# 7. SUMMARY
# ============================================================

The source architecture exists so the domain can remain:
- policy-aware
- replaceable
- governable
- resilient
- operationally controllable



# ------------------------------------------------------------
# FILE: /data/data/com.termux/files/home/01.civilization-system/03.business-os/020.architecture/250.public-company-intelligence/0202507_PUBLIC_COMPANY_INTELLIGENCE_REVIEW_ARCHITECTURE.md
# ------------------------------------------------------------

# ============================================================
# PUBLIC COMPANY INTELLIGENCE REVIEW ARCHITECTURE
# ============================================================

status: draft
system: business-os
domain: public-company-intelligence
layer: 020.architecture
owner: Boss
prepared_by: Zero

# ============================================================
# 0. REVIEW ARCHITECTURE SUMMARY
# ============================================================

This domain is review-oriented rather than blind-auto-finalizing.

Because company identity, officer identity, title normalization,
and source conflict may contain ambiguity, review must exist as
a first-class architectural concern.

# ============================================================
# 1. WHY REVIEW IS REQUIRED
# ============================================================

review_is_required_because:
- public-source values may conflict
- company names may have ambiguity
- officer names may have ambiguity
- titles may vary across sources
- strong-looking matches may still be wrong
- irreversible merge damage must be avoided

# ============================================================
# 2. REVIEW TARGETS
# ============================================================

review_targets:
- ambiguous company match
- ambiguous officer match
- conflicting public titles
- risky normalized-company-key merge
- risky normalized-officer-key merge
- suspicious profile field change
- weak-evidence update proposal

# ============================================================
# 3. REVIEW INPUTS
# ============================================================

review_inputs:
- match_score
- confidence_level
- source disagreement
- field conflict
- profile change severity
- normalization ambiguity

# ============================================================
# 4. REVIEW OUTPUTS
# ============================================================

review_outputs:
- approved
- rejected
- merged
- ignored
- escalated
- held for more evidence

# ============================================================
# 5. AUTO-FINALIZATION BOUNDARY
# ============================================================

safe_auto_behavior_may_include:
- low-risk profile refresh with strong evidence
- low-risk normalization where ambiguity is low
- low-risk freshness updates

not_safe_for_blind_auto_finalization:
- high-ambiguity company merge
- high-ambiguity officer merge
- major profile conflict across sources
- destructive interpretation of weak signals

# ============================================================
# 6. REVIEW QUEUE AS DOMAIN STRUCTURE
# ============================================================

The review queue is not an afterthought.

It is part of the core domain because it preserves:
- correctness
- reversibility
- trust
- operational explainability

# ============================================================
# 7. SUMMARY
# ============================================================

The review architecture ensures that this domain remains:
- useful
- safe
- auditable
- human-correctable
without pretending that all public-data matching is certainty.

# FILE: /data/data/com.termux/files/home/01.civilization-system/03.business-os/030.model/040.persona/010303040000001_BUSINESS_PERSONA_ACCESS_REF_MODEL.md
# ------------------------------------------------------------

# ============================================================
# BUSINESS PERSONA ACCESS REF MODEL
# ============================================================

status: canonical
layer: 030.model
system: business-os
owner: Boss
prepared_by: Zero

purpose:
Reference Persona access state inside BusinessOS.

role:
This model is a synchronized reference model.
Truth belongs to PersonaOS.
BusinessOS must not directly author Persona truth here.

BusinessOS is primarily user-scoped.
Company context must not be part of the default identity of this model.
Company context may be attached only for ERP-send-capable app flows
when needed as outbound integration context.

primary_key:
- business_persona_access_ref_id

natural_key:
- business_user_id
- persona_id

fields:
- business_persona_access_ref_id
- business_user_id
- persona_id
- persona_code
- access_status
- access_scope
- access_granted_at
- access_expires_at
- erp_company_context_id
- source_sync_event_id
- source_sync_version
- correlation_id
- synced_at
- created_at
- updated_at

access_status_enum:
- pending
- active
- suspended
- revoked
- expired

access_scope_examples:
- assistant.read
- assistant.chat
- assistant.execute_limited
- assistant.execute_extended

rules:
- only Persona-originated sync results may change access_status
- BusinessOS may cache and read this model
- BusinessOS must treat expired and revoked as unusable
- erp_company_context_id is optional and must not be part of the default truth identity
- correlation_id must trace back to Persona sync result when applicable



# ------------------------------------------------------------
# FILE: /data/data/com.termux/files/home/01.civilization-system/03.business-os/030.model/040.persona/010303040000002_BUSINESS_PERSONA_LICENSE_REF_MODEL.md
# ------------------------------------------------------------

# ============================================================
# BUSINESS PERSONA LICENSE REF MODEL
# ============================================================

status: canonical
layer: 030.model
system: business-os
owner: Boss
prepared_by: Zero

purpose:
Reference Persona license or usage permission state inside BusinessOS.

role:
This model represents Business-visible permission state returned by PersonaOS.

BusinessOS is primarily user-scoped.
Company context may be attached only when ERP-send-capable app behavior
requires outbound company-scoped payload construction.

primary_key:
- business_persona_license_ref_id

natural_key:
- business_user_id
- persona_id

fields:
- business_persona_license_ref_id
- business_user_id
- persona_id
- usage_permission_status
- granted_scope
- denied_scope
- revoked_reason
- effective_from
- effective_until
- erp_company_context_id
- source_sync_event_id
- source_sync_version
- correlation_id
- synced_at
- created_at
- updated_at

usage_permission_status_enum:
- pending
- granted
- denied
- revoked
- expired

rules:
- permission and trust are separate
- granted does not imply unrestricted exposure
- BusinessOS must combine this model with trust ref
- PersonaOS remains truth holder
- erp_company_context_id is optional and must not be part of the default truth identity

- expired

- privileged

- erp_company_context_id is optional and not part of the natural key

# FILE: /data/data/com.termux/files/home/01.civilization-system/03.business-os/030.model/140.business-ai-worker/0301430_BUSINESS_AI_WORKER_PHYSICAL_SCHEMA_FIXED.md
# ------------------------------------------------------------

# ============================================================
# BUSINESS AI WORKER PHYSICAL SCHEMA FIXED
# ============================================================

status: canonical
layer: model
domain: business-ai-worker
system: business-os
owner: Boss
prepared_by: Zero

purpose:
Defines the fixed physical schema set
for Business AI Worker foundation-side persistence.

schema_name:
business_os

# ============================================================
# 1. TABLE SET
# ============================================================

tables:
- ai_worker_template
- ai_worker_capability_profile
- ai_worker_employment
- ai_worker_assignment
- ai_worker_capacity_slot
- ai_worker_subscription
- ai_worker_lending
- ai_worker_reservation
- ai_worker_company_terminology
- ai_worker_company_knowledge_entry
- ai_worker_disclaimer
- ai_worker_consent
- ai_worker_advisory_session
- ai_worker_execution_task
- ai_worker_output_handoff
- ai_worker_usage_log
- ai_worker_audit_trace

# ============================================================
# 2. ai_worker_template
# ============================================================

primary_key:
- worker_template_id

columns:
- worker_template_id: uuid
- template_name: text
- default_rank: text
- default_knowledge_depth: text
- is_active: boolean
- created_at: timestamptz
- updated_at: timestamptz

# ============================================================
# 3. ai_worker_capability_profile
# ============================================================

primary_key:
- capability_profile_id

columns:
- capability_profile_id: uuid
- worker_template_id: uuid
- specialty: text
- knowledge_depth: text
- supports_advisory: boolean
- supports_execution: boolean
- supports_embedded_app_work: boolean
- supports_forecasting: boolean
- supports_management_assistance: boolean
- supports_improvement_assistance: boolean
- created_at: timestamptz
- updated_at: timestamptz

# ============================================================
# 4. ai_worker_employment
# ============================================================

primary_key:
- employment_id

columns:
- employment_id: uuid
- company_id: uuid
- worker_id: uuid
- worker_template_id: uuid
- subscribed_rank: text
- employment_status: text
- started_at: timestamptz
- ended_at: timestamptz
- created_at: timestamptz
- updated_at: timestamptz

indexes:
- company_id
- worker_id
- subscribed_rank
- employment_status

# ============================================================
# 5. ai_worker_assignment
# ============================================================

primary_key:
- assignment_id

columns:
- assignment_id: uuid
- company_id: uuid
- worker_id: uuid
- assignment_scope_type: text
- assignment_scope_id: text
- app_surface: text
- assigned_role_name: text
- assigned_at: timestamptz
- released_at: timestamptz
- created_at: timestamptz

indexes:
- company_id
- worker_id
- app_surface

# ============================================================
# 6. ai_worker_capacity_slot
# ============================================================

primary_key:
- capacity_slot_id

columns:
- capacity_slot_id: uuid
- company_id: uuid
- subscribed_rank: text
- slot_status: text
- current_lending_id: uuid
- reserved_for_reservation_id: uuid
- activated_at: timestamptz
- released_at: timestamptz
- created_at: timestamptz
- updated_at: timestamptz

indexes:
- company_id
- subscribed_rank
- slot_status

# ============================================================
# 7. ai_worker_subscription
# ============================================================

primary_key:
- subscription_id

columns:
- subscription_id: uuid
- company_id: uuid
- subscribed_rank: text
- subscribed_capacity: integer
- active_from: timestamptz
- active_until: timestamptz
- billing_status: text
- auto_renew: boolean
- created_at: timestamptz
- updated_at: timestamptz

indexes:
- company_id
- subscribed_rank
- billing_status

# ============================================================
# 8. ai_worker_lending
# ============================================================

primary_key:
- lending_id

columns:
- lending_id: uuid
- company_id: uuid
- worker_id: uuid
- capacity_slot_id: uuid
- granted_rank: text
- activity_mode: text
- world_scope: text
- specialty: text
- knowledge_depth: text
- app_surface: text
- task_summary: text
- actor_id: uuid
- lending_status: text

# FILE: /data/data/com.termux/files/home/01.civilization-system/03.business-os/030.model/210.business-core/0302100_BUSINESS_USER_SCOPE_MODEL.md
# ------------------------------------------------------------

# ============================================================
# BUSINESS USER SCOPE MODEL
# ============================================================

status: canonical
layer: 030.model
system: business-os
owner: Boss
prepared_by: Zero

purpose:
Define the official user-scope truth model of BusinessOS.

BusinessOS is primarily user-scoped.
It hosts user-oriented small business applications
with app-level paid features.

Some BusinessOS apps may send real operational data to ERP,
for example:
- travel expense data
- business card data

When sending to ERP,
BusinessOS attaches company context,
because ERP is company-scoped.


# ============================================================
# 1. PRIMARY TRUTH HOLDER
# ============================================================

The default truth holder of BusinessOS is the user.

BusinessOS must not treat:
- company
- company tenant
- enterprise org

as the default top-level truth holder.


# ============================================================
# 2. USER-SCOPE DOMAINS
# ============================================================

Typical user-scope domains may include:
- travel expense draft/entry
- business card entry/management
- contacts
- lightweight sales tracking
- lightweight inventory notes
- lightweight customer notes
- task and schedule support
- personal business utilities


# ============================================================
# 3. ERP-SEND EXCEPTION
# ============================================================

ERP-send is an exception path.

When a BusinessOS app sends data to ERP,
the payload must attach:
- company_id
- user/employee linkage where required
- app context
- payload type
- mapping profile where required

This does not change BusinessOS primary truth scope.


# ============================================================
# 4. FINAL RULE
# ============================================================

BusinessOS truth is primarily user-scoped.

Core summary:

- user is the default truth holder
- apps are user-oriented
- ERP-send adds company context only at send time



# ------------------------------------------------------------
# FILE: /data/data/com.termux/files/home/01.civilization-system/03.business-os/030.model/210.business-core/0302101_BUSINESS_WORKSPACE_MODEL.md
# ------------------------------------------------------------

# ============================================================
# BUSINESS WORKSPACE MODEL
# ============================================================

status: canonical
layer: 030.model
system: business-os
owner: Boss
prepared_by: Zero

purpose:
Define the official workspace model of BusinessOS.

BusinessOS is primarily user-scoped.
A workspace is a user-centered business app context,
not a company truth container.

BusinessOS may support app-level paid features.
Some apps may send real operational data to ERP.
When sending to ERP, BusinessOS attaches company context
because ERP is company-scoped.

BusinessOS itself does not treat company as
the default top-level truth holder.


# ============================================================
# 1. ROLE
# ============================================================

A workspace is the primary operating context
for BusinessOS apps.

It groups:
- user-owned app data
- app settings
- app memberships where relevant
- ERP-send capability flags where relevant

A workspace is not equivalent to:
- legal company truth
- ERP company-scoped truth context
- enterprise master truth


# ============================================================
# 2. CORE FIELDS
# ============================================================

recommended_fields:
- workspace_id
- owner_user_id
- workspace_code
- workspace_name
- workspace_status
- default_app_scope
- erp_send_capable_flag
- created_at
- updated_at


# ============================================================
# 3. ERP CONTEXT
# ============================================================

A workspace may optionally carry ERP-send context hints,
but these are not default truth identity.

optional_fields:
- default_company_id_for_erp_send
- erp_mapping_profile_id
- erp_send_policy_id

These fields are used only when:
- a BusinessOS app sends real data to ERP
- the ERP payload must be company-scoped


# ============================================================
# 4. FINAL RULE
# ============================================================

BusinessOS workspace truth is user/workspace-scoped.

Core summary:

- workspace is a user-centered app container
- workspace is not a company-scope root truth holder
- company context is attached only for ERP-send flows

- granted_at
- revoked_at
- created_at
- updated_at

grant_mode examples:
- allow
- deny
- ask_each_time


# ============================================================
# 3. APP EFFECTIVE ACCESS DECISION
# ============================================================

core_fields:
- app_effective_access_decision_id
- user_ref
- app_id
- resource_domain
- action_type
- requested_scope_ref
- granted_scope_ref
- system_policy_ref
- effective_decision
- decision_reason_summary
- decided_at
- created_at

effective_decision examples:
- allowed
- denied
- ask_each_time
- blocked_by_policy
- unresolved_policy


# ============================================================
# 4. APP RESOURCE DOMAIN PROFILE
# ============================================================

core_fields:
- app_resource_domain_profile_id
- app_id
- resource_domain
- default_access_mode
- export_allowed
- delete_allowed
- profile_status
- created_at
- updated_at


# ============================================================
# 5. FINAL MODEL MAP RULE
# ============================================================

This model map is the minimum support set
for BusinessOS app access control.

Core summary:

- app requested scope is explicit
- user granted scope is explicit
- effective access decision is explicit
- resource domain profile is explicit

- correlation_id
- dead_letter_status
- source_failure_ref
- dead_letter_summary
- source_state_version
- recorded_at
- created_at
- updated_at

dead_letter_status_enum:
- quarantined
- restored
- invalidated
- archived

truth_boundary:
Business shared dead letter truth belongs to BusinessOS cross-cutting-completion domain.

# FILE: /data/data/com.termux/files/home/01.civilization-system/03.business-os/030.model/250.public-company-intelligence/0302502_PUBLIC_SOURCE_REGISTRY_MODEL.md
# ------------------------------------------------------------

# ============================================================
# PUBLIC SOURCE REGISTRY MODEL
# ============================================================

status: draft
system: business-os
domain: public-company-intelligence
layer: 030.model
owner: Boss
prepared_by: Zero

entity: public_source_registry

# ============================================================
# 0. PURPOSE
# ============================================================

The public_source_registry entity defines which public sources
are available to this domain and under what governance state
they may be used.

It prevents source access rules from being scattered across
batch code and normalization logic.

# ============================================================
# 1. MAIN FIELDS
# ============================================================

main_fields:
- public_source_registry_id
- source_code
- source_name
- source_type
- base_domain
- access_method
- robots_policy_status
- terms_checked_at
- rate_limit_rule
- attribution_required
- enabled
- disabled_reason
- owner_note
- created_at
- updated_at

# ============================================================
# 2. FIELD MEANING
# ============================================================

field_meaning:
- source_code:
    stable internal code for the source
- source_name:
    human-readable source name
- source_type:
    official-site / registry / ir / permitted-public-source / other
- base_domain:
    source domain summary
- access_method:
    api / crawl / import / manual-seeded / other-governed-method
- robots_policy_status:
    policy review result summary
- terms_checked_at:
    last reviewed time for policy understanding
- rate_limit_rule:
    operational throttle summary
- attribution_required:
    whether downstream attribution must be retained
- enabled:
    whether the source can be used by jobs
- disabled_reason:
    why the source is unavailable
- owner_note:
    governance memo without embedding business truth

# ============================================================
# 3. MODEL RULES
# ============================================================

model_rules:
- disabled source must be skippable by batch planning
- source metadata must not be inferred from consumer apps
- policy state must be visible to operations
- source identity must remain stable even if access details change

# ============================================================
# 4. NON-GOALS
# ============================================================

non_goals:
- no raw payload storage here
- no profile field storage here
- no fetch history storage here

# FILE: /data/data/com.termux/files/home/01.civilization-system/03.business-os/030.model/250.public-company-intelligence/0302503_COMPANY_PUBLIC_SOURCE_SNAPSHOT_MODEL.md
# ------------------------------------------------------------

# ============================================================
# COMPANY PUBLIC SOURCE SNAPSHOT MODEL
# ============================================================

status: draft
system: business-os
domain: public-company-intelligence
layer: 030.model
owner: Boss
prepared_by: Zero

entity: company_public_source_snapshot

# ============================================================
# 0. PURPOSE
# ============================================================

company_public_source_snapshot preserves raw public-source
evidence relevant to company-level facts.

This entity exists so that:
- public evidence is reproducible
- normalization can be re-run
- source-backed audit remains possible
- parse improvements can be applied later

# ============================================================
# 1. MAIN FIELDS
# ============================================================

main_fields:
- company_public_source_snapshot_id
- source_registry_id
- source_reference
- source_url
- source_document_type
- source_published_at
- fetched_at
- fetch_status
- http_status
- raw_title
- raw_body
- raw_payload_json
- content_hash
- detected_company_name
- detected_corporate_number
- detected_security_code
- parse_state
- parse_error_reason
- created_at

# ============================================================
# 2. FIELD MEANING
# ============================================================

field_meaning:
- source_registry_id:
    which governed source produced this snapshot
- source_reference:
    source-side reference or document identity
- source_url:
    retrieval URL when applicable
- source_document_type:
    page / filing / ir-page / company-page / registry-record / other
- source_published_at:
    source-side publication or update time when available
- fetched_at:
    actual retrieval time
- fetch_status:
    queued / success / partial_success / failed / blocked / skipped
- http_status:
    transport-layer status when applicable
- raw_title:
    preserved source title or heading
- raw_body:
    preserved raw text body when stored as text
- raw_payload_json:
    preserved structured payload when structured format exists
- content_hash:
    duplicate and change detection support
- detected_company_name:
    lightweight extracted company hint from raw data
- detected_corporate_number:
    lightweight extracted corporate-number hint
- detected_security_code:
    lightweight extracted security-code hint
- parse_state:
    parse result state
- parse_error_reason:
    parse failure explanation when relevant

# ============================================================
# 3. MODEL RULES
# ============================================================

model_rules:
- raw snapshot must remain raw enough for reprocessing
- snapshot may exist even when parse fails
- fetch failure and parse failure are distinct
- content_hash supports duplicate-safe processing
- source_reference and fetched_at are mandatory trace points

# ============================================================
# 4. NON-GOALS
# ============================================================

non_goals:
- no final company truth here
- no merge finalization here
- no consumer-oriented display ownership here

officer_public_source_snapshot preserves raw public-source
evidence relevant to officer-level facts.

officer extraction and officer ambiguity often need distinct
handling and later reprocessing.

main_fields:
- officer_public_source_snapshot_id
- source_registry_id
- source_reference

- raw_officer_name

- raw_section_name
- raw_payload_json
- content_hash
- parse_state
- parse_error_reason
- created_at

# ============================================================

# ============================================================

    company name as expressed in source context
- raw_officer_name:
    officer name as expressed in source context
- raw_title:
    officer title as expressed in source context
- raw_section_name:
    source structural hint such as officer section or organization block
- raw_payload_json:
    preserved structured officer extraction context
- content_hash:
    deduplication and change-detection support
- parse_state:
    officer parse status
- parse_error_reason:
    officer parse failure explanation

# ============================================================
# 3. MODEL RULES
# ============================================================

model_rules:
- raw officer values must remain preserved
- officer parsing may succeed even when company match is unresolved
- officer ambiguity must not be hidden at snapshot level
- raw title must remain available for later dictionary improvements

# ============================================================

# ============================================================

non_goals:
- no canonical officer identity finalization here
- no title-rank finalization here

# ============================================================
# COMPANY PUBLIC PROFILE MODEL
# ============================================================

status: draft
system: business-os
domain: public-company-intelligence
layer: 030.model
owner: Boss
prepared_by: Zero

entity: company_public_profile

# ============================================================
# 0. PURPOSE
# ============================================================

company_public_profile is the reusable normalized public-facing
company profile built from governed public sources.

It is intended for downstream reference by applications such as
NameCardManager while preserving source traceability,
freshness visibility, and review-aware semantics.

# ============================================================
# 1. MAIN FIELDS
# ============================================================

main_fields:
- company_public_profile_id
- normalized_company_key
- canonical_company_name
- company_name_kana
- corporate_number
- security_code
- website_url
- ir_url
- phone_number
- postal_address
- prefecture
- country_code
- industry_primary
- industry_secondary
- listed_status
- market_name
- company_status
- business_summary
- representative_name
- latest_public_update_at
- freshness_score
- normalization_state
- confidence_level
- review_required
- visibility_scope
- created_at
- updated_at

# ============================================================
# 2. FIELD MEANING
# ============================================================

field_meaning:
- normalized_company_key:
    normalized identity-support key for same-company handling
- canonical_company_name:
    selected normalized public company display name
- company_name_kana:
    optional kana support when available and governed
- corporate_number:
    strong public identity support field when available
- security_code:
    market-related identity support field when available
- website_url:
    selected public website
- ir_url:
    selected investor-relations URL when applicable
- phone_number:
    selected public phone number
- postal_address:
    selected public address
- industry_primary:
    selected primary industry expression
- industry_secondary:
    optional additional industry expression
- listed_status:
    listed / non-listed / unknown
- market_name:
    market segment when applicable
- company_status:
    active / inactive / unknown
- business_summary:
    normalized public business summary
- representative_name:
    public representative name when supported
- latest_public_update_at:
    latest known public-source update reference
- freshness_score:
    freshness-support indicator for consumer use
- normalization_state:
    profile readiness state
- confidence_level:
    profile confidence summary
- review_required:
    whether caution or review remains necessary
- visibility_scope:
    public-source based visibility metadata

# ============================================================
# 3. MODEL RULES
# ============================================================

model_rules:
- profile fields must remain source-backed
- profile must not overwrite internal relationship truth
- normalized_company_key is not the same as raw source expression
- review_required must remain visible to downstream consumers
- confidence_level summarizes trust posture, not perfect certainty

# ============================================================
# 4. NON-GOALS
# ============================================================

non_goals:
- no internal notes here
- no subjective sales judgement here
- no hidden private-relationship inference here

# ============================================================

# ============================================================

company_officer_profile is the reusable normalized public
officer profile associated with a company public profile.

It exists separately because officer identity, officer title,
and officer ambiguity require different normalization and
review patterns than company identity.

# ============================================================

- officer_role_type
- representative_flag

- latest_source_at
- confidence_level
- normalization_state
- review_required
- created_at
- updated_at

# ============================================================
# 2. FIELD MEANING
# ============================================================

field_meaning:
- company_public_profile_id:
    owning company profile relationship
- normalized_officer_key:
    normalized identity-support key for officer handling
- canonical_officer_name:
    selected normalized public officer name
- canonical_title:
    selected normalized title
- title_rank:
    normalized title hierarchy support
- officer_role_type:
    role-class support such as director / executive / representative / other
- representative_flag:
    whether the officer is treated as representative in public profile logic

- latest_source_at:

    officer normalization readiness state
- review_required:
    ambiguity or caution indicator

- officer profile must stay linked to company profile

- officer ambiguity must remain reviewable
