# ============================================================
# PUBLIC COMPANY INTELLIGENCE SUPPORT API EXACT PAYLOAD
# ============================================================

status: draft
system: business-os
domain: public-company-intelligence
layer: 120.implementation
owner: Boss
prepared_by: Zero

# ============================================================
# 0. PURPOSE
# ============================================================

This document fixes the exact support payload shapes for
consumer applications such as NameCardManager.

The goal is to make consumer integration implementation-ready
without collapsing source traceability, confidence visibility,
or review visibility.

# ============================================================
# 1. COMMON RESPONSE PRINCIPLES
# ============================================================

common_response_principles:
- all support responses are assistive
- low-confidence must remain visible
- review_required must remain visible
- freshness must remain visible
- source-backed fields remain distinguishable from consumer-owned fields
- response shape should remain stable across consumers

common_response_envelope:
- request_id
- result_code
- result_message
- generated_at
- data

result_code_candidates:
- OK
- PARTIAL_OK
- NOT_FOUND
- REVIEW_REQUIRED
- INVALID_REQUEST
- SOURCE_UNAVAILABLE
- INTERNAL_ERROR

# ============================================================
# 2. COMPANY GROUPING SUPPORT
# ============================================================

api_name:
- public-company-intelligence/company-grouping-support

purpose:
- help consuming app find likely same-company candidates

request_json:
{
  "consumer_app": "NameCardManager",
  "request_id": "string",
  "company_input": {
    "raw_company_name": "string",
    "website_url": "string|null",
    "phone_number": "string|null",
    "postal_address": "string|null",
    "corporate_number": "string|null",
    "security_code": "string|null"
  },
  "options": {
    "max_candidates": 10,
    "include_low_confidence": true,
    "include_review_required": true
  }
}

response_json:
{
  "request_id": "string",
  "result_code": "OK",
  "result_message": "success",
  "generated_at": "ISO-8601",
  "data": {
    "input_echo": {
      "raw_company_name": "string",
      "website_url": "string|null",
      "phone_number": "string|null",
      "postal_address": "string|null",
      "corporate_number": "string|null",
      "security_code": "string|null"
    },
    "normalized_company_key_hint": "string|null",
    "candidate_count": 2,
    "candidates": [
      {
        "company_public_profile_id": "uuid-or-string",
        "canonical_company_name": "string",
        "normalized_company_key": "string",
        "corporate_number": "string|null",
        "website_url": "string|null",
        "phone_number": "string|null",
        "postal_address": "string|null",
        "listed_status": "listed|non-listed|unknown",
        "confidence_level": "high|medium|low|unknown",
        "review_required": false,
        "match_score": 0.93,
        "match_reasons": [
          "company_name_similarity",
          "website_domain_match"
        ],
        "freshness_summary": {
          "latest_public_update_at": "ISO-8601|null",
          "freshness_score": 88,
          "freshness_state": "fresh|stale|unknown"
        }
      }
    ]
  }
}

# ============================================================
# 3. MIGRATION ENRICHMENT SUPPORT
# ============================================================

api_name:
- public-company-intelligence/migration-enrichment-support

purpose:
- help enrich imported company and officer data after migration

request_json:
{
  "consumer_app": "NameCardManager",
  "request_id": "string",
  "import_context": {
    "raw_company_name": "string",
    "raw_officer_name": "string|null",
    "raw_title": "string|null",
    "website_url": "string|null",
    "phone_number": "string|null",
    "postal_address": "string|null"
  },
  "options": {
    "include_company_candidates": true,
    "include_officer_candidates": true,
    "include_missing_field_hints": true,
    "max_company_candidates": 5,
    "max_officer_candidates": 5
  }
}

response_json:
{
  "request_id": "string",
  "result_code": "OK",
  "result_message": "success",
  "generated_at": "ISO-8601",
  "data": {
    "company_candidates": [
      {
        "company_public_profile_id": "uuid-or-string",
        "canonical_company_name": "string",
        "normalized_company_key": "string",
        "corporate_number": "string|null",
        "website_url": "string|null",
        "phone_number": "string|null",
        "postal_address": "string|null",
        "industry_primary": "string|null",
        "business_summary": "string|null",
        "confidence_level": "high|medium|low|unknown",
        "review_required": false,
        "match_score": 0.91,
        "freshness_summary": {
          "latest_public_update_at": "ISO-8601|null",
          "freshness_score": 84,
          "freshness_state": "fresh|stale|unknown"
        }
      }
    ],
    "officer_candidates": [
      {
        "company_officer_profile_id": "uuid-or-string",
        "company_public_profile_id": "uuid-or-string",
        "canonical_officer_name": "string",
        "canonical_title": "string|null",
        "representative_flag": false,
        "confidence_level": "high|medium|low|unknown",
        "review_required": true,
        "match_score": 0.64,
        "match_reasons": [
          "name_similarity_only"
        ]
      }
    ],
    "missing_field_hints": [
      "corporate_number_missing",
      "website_url_missing"
    ]
  }
}

# ============================================================
# 4. PUBLICATION PREFLIGHT SUPPORT
# ============================================================

api_name:
- public-company-intelligence/publication-preflight-support

purpose:
- provide public-information support before publication-related action

request_json:
{
  "consumer_app": "NameCardManager",
  "request_id": "string",
  "target_company": {
    "raw_company_name": "string",
    "canonical_company_name": "string|null",
    "corporate_number": "string|null",
    "website_url": "string|null",
    "phone_number": "string|null",
    "postal_address": "string|null"
  },
  "options": {
    "include_officer_support": true,
    "include_freshness_warning": true,
    "include_review_warning": true
  }
}

response_json:
{
  "request_id": "string",
  "result_code": "OK",
  "result_message": "success",
  "generated_at": "ISO-8601",
  "data": {
    "matched_company_public_profile": {
      "company_public_profile_id": "uuid-or-string",
      "canonical_company_name": "string",
      "corporate_number": "string|null",
      "website_url": "string|null",
      "phone_number": "string|null",
      "postal_address": "string|null",
      "confidence_level": "high|medium|low|unknown",
      "review_required": false
    },
    "consistency_checks": [
      {
        "field_name": "corporate_number",
        "status": "match|mismatch|missing|unknown",
        "input_value": "string|null",
        "public_value": "string|null",
        "warning_code": "none|mismatch|missing_public_value|missing_input_value"
      },
      {
        "field_name": "website_url",
        "status": "match|mismatch|missing|unknown",
        "input_value": "string|null",
        "public_value": "string|null",
        "warning_code": "none|mismatch|missing_public_value|missing_input_value"
      }
    ],
    "officer_support": [
      {
        "company_officer_profile_id": "uuid-or-string",
        "canonical_officer_name": "string",
        "canonical_title": "string|null",
        "representative_flag": true,
        "confidence_level": "high|medium|low|unknown",
        "review_required": false
      }
    ],
    "freshness_summary": {
      "latest_public_update_at": "ISO-8601|null",
      "freshness_score": 79,
      "freshness_state": "fresh|stale|unknown"
    },
    "warnings": [
      "public_profile_stale",
      "review_required_for_company_match"
    ]
  }
}

# ============================================================
# 5. PUBLIC COMPANY VIEW SUPPORT
# ============================================================

api_name:
- public-company-intelligence/public-company-view-support

purpose:
- provide source-backed public company summary for company view

request_json:
{
  "consumer_app": "NameCardManager",
  "request_id": "string",
  "lookup": {
    "company_public_profile_id": "uuid-or-string|null",
    "raw_company_name": "string|null",
    "corporate_number": "string|null",
    "website_url": "string|null"
  },
  "options": {
    "include_officers": true,
    "include_business_summary": true,
    "include_selected_sources": true
  }
}

response_json:
{
  "request_id": "string",
  "result_code": "OK",
  "result_message": "success",
  "generated_at": "ISO-8601",
  "data": {
    "company_profile": {
      "company_public_profile_id": "uuid-or-string",
      "canonical_company_name": "string",
      "company_name_kana": "string|null",
      "corporate_number": "string|null",
      "security_code": "string|null",
      "website_url": "string|null",
      "ir_url": "string|null",
      "phone_number": "string|null",
      "postal_address": "string|null",
      "industry_primary": "string|null",
      "listed_status": "listed|non-listed|unknown",
      "market_name": "string|null",
      "business_summary": "string|null",
      "representative_name": "string|null",
      "confidence_level": "high|medium|low|unknown",
      "review_required": false
    },
    "officers": [
      {
        "company_officer_profile_id": "uuid-or-string",
        "canonical_officer_name": "string",
        "canonical_title": "string|null",
        "representative_flag": false,
        "confidence_level": "high|medium|low|unknown",
        "review_required": false
      }
    ],
    "freshness_summary": {
      "latest_public_update_at": "ISO-8601|null",
      "freshness_score": 80,
      "freshness_state": "fresh|stale|unknown"
    },
    "selected_sources": [
      {
        "field_name": "canonical_company_name",
        "source_type": "official-site|registry|ir|other",
        "source_reference": "string",
        "fetched_at": "ISO-8601"
      }
    ]
  }
}

# ============================================================
# 6. OFFICER CANDIDATE SUPPORT
# ============================================================

api_name:
- public-company-intelligence/officer-candidate-support

purpose:
- provide officer candidate lookup for a given company context

request_json:
{
  "consumer_app": "NameCardManager",
  "request_id": "string",
  "company_context": {
    "company_public_profile_id": "uuid-or-string|null",
    "raw_company_name": "string|null",
    "corporate_number": "string|null"
  },
  "officer_input": {
    "raw_officer_name": "string",
    "raw_title": "string|null"
  },
  "options": {
    "max_candidates": 5,
    "include_review_required": true
  }
}

response_json:
{
  "request_id": "string",
  "result_code": "OK",
  "result_message": "success",
  "generated_at": "ISO-8601",
  "data": {
    "candidate_count": 2,
    "candidates": [
      {
        "company_officer_profile_id": "uuid-or-string",
        "company_public_profile_id": "uuid-or-string",
        "canonical_officer_name": "string",
        "canonical_title": "string|null",
        "representative_flag": false,
        "confidence_level": "high|medium|low|unknown",
        "review_required": true,
        "match_score": 0.67,
        "match_reasons": [
          "name_similarity",
          "same_company_context"
        ]
      }
    ]
  }
}

# ============================================================
# 7. LIGHTWEIGHT REFRESH REQUEST
# ============================================================

api_name:
- public-company-intelligence/refresh-request

purpose:
- queue lightweight refresh support request without forcing heavy synchronous retrieval

request_json:
{
  "consumer_app": "NameCardManager",
  "request_id": "string",
  "refresh_target": {
    "raw_company_name": "string",
    "corporate_number": "string|null",
    "website_url": "string|null"
  },
  "reason_code": "new_company_detected|migration_completed|preflight_requested|manual_refresh_requested"
}

response_json:
{
  "request_id": "string",
  "result_code": "OK",
  "result_message": "queued",
  "generated_at": "ISO-8601",
  "data": {
    "queued": true,
    "queue_type": "lightweight_refresh_request",
    "accepted_reason_code": "new_company_detected|migration_completed|preflight_requested|manual_refresh_requested"
  }
}

# ============================================================
# 8. COMMON ENUMS
# ============================================================

confidence_level:
- high
- medium
- low
- unknown

freshness_state:
- fresh
- stale
- unknown

consistency_status:
- match
- mismatch
- missing
- unknown

# ============================================================
# 9. IMPLEMENTATION RULES
# ============================================================

implementation_rules:
- request and response field names must be fixed before app coupling
- confidence_level must always be returned when candidate semantics exist
- review_required must always be returned when ambiguity semantics exist
- freshness_summary must always be returned for public profile support
- support APIs must remain assistive and non-destructive
- source-backed selected_sources may be omitted only when options exclude them

# ============================================================
# 10. SUMMARY
# ============================================================

These exact payloads make the Public Company Intelligence domain
implementation-ready for consumer support integration,
especially for NameCardManager grouping, migration enrichment,
publication preflight, company view support, and officer lookup.

# ============================================================
# PUBLIC COMPANY INTELLIGENCE VIEW AND ENDPOINT EXACT CONTRACT
# ============================================================

status: draft
system: business-os
domain: public-company-intelligence
db_position: persona-db / business schema
layer: 120.implementation
owner: Boss
prepared_by: Zero

# ============================================================
# 0. PURPOSE
# ============================================================

This document fixes the exact internal read views and support
endpoints for Public Company Intelligence.

This domain is implemented on the Persona-side database and
uses the existing business schema.

The goal is to make:
- DB read-side design
- application integration
- API implementation
- consumer coupling
stable before source-code implementation begins.

# ============================================================
# 1. CONTRACT PRINCIPLES
# ============================================================

contract_principles:
- read views are internal BusinessOS read models
- support endpoints are assistive contracts
- view names are stable and explicit
- endpoint names are stable and explicit
- confidence and review visibility are mandatory
- freshness visibility is mandatory
- public/private boundary must survive the contract
- all application-side consumers are Persona-side applications

# ============================================================
# 2. INTERNAL READ VIEWS
# ============================================================

# ------------------------------------------------------------
# 2-1. business.v_pci_company_public_profile_latest
# ------------------------------------------------------------

view_name:
- business.v_pci_company_public_profile_latest

purpose:
- latest reusable company public profile read model

columns:
- company_public_profile_id
- normalized_company_key
- canonical_company_name
- company_name_kana
- corporate_number
- security_code
- website_url
- ir_url
- phone_number
- postal_address
- prefecture
- country_code
- industry_primary
- industry_secondary
- listed_status
- market_name
- company_status
- business_summary
- representative_name
- latest_public_update_at
- freshness_score
- freshness_state
- confidence_level
- review_required
- updated_at

primary_lookup_keys:
- company_public_profile_id
- normalized_company_key
- corporate_number
- website_url

# ------------------------------------------------------------
# 2-2. business.v_pci_company_officer_profile_latest
# ------------------------------------------------------------

view_name:
- business.v_pci_company_officer_profile_latest

- canonical_title
- title_rank

- representative_flag

- review_required
- updated_at

- company_public_profile_id
- normalized_officer_key

# ------------------------------------------------------------

- failure_count
- warning_count
- created_at

primary_lookup_keys:
- company_batch_job_id
- job_status
- chunk_key

# ============================================================
# 3. SUPPORT ENDPOINTS
# ============================================================

base_path:
- /business-os/public-company-intelligence

endpoints:
- POST /business-os/public-company-intelligence/company-grouping-support
- POST /business-os/public-company-intelligence/migration-enrichment-support
- POST /business-os/public-company-intelligence/publication-preflight-support
- POST /business-os/public-company-intelligence/public-company-view-support
- POST /business-os/public-company-intelligence/officer-candidate-support
- POST /business-os/public-company-intelligence/refresh-request
- GET  /business-os/public-company-intelligence/review-queue/open
- GET  /business-os/public-company-intelligence/batch-jobs/latest
- POST /business-os/public-company-intelligence/review-queue/action

# ============================================================
# 4. IMPLEMENTATION RULES
# ============================================================

implementation_rules:
- all endpoint paths are fixed strings
- all views are created in business schema
- all response envelopes keep result_code/result_message/generated_at/data
- support endpoints are POST when request body matching is needed
- monitoring and queue listing endpoints are GET
- all timestamps use ISO-8601
- exact request/response shape changes require explicit versioning decision

# ============================================================
# 5. SUMMARY
# ============================================================

These exact view and endpoint contracts give the domain a fixed
integration surface for Persona-side applications while keeping
the storage position inside the existing business schema.

# ------------------------------------------------------------

# ============================================================
# PUBLIC COMPANY INTELLIGENCE PHYSICAL DDL SPEC
# ============================================================

status: draft
system: business-os
domain: public-company-intelligence
db_position: persona-db / business schema
layer: 120.implementation
owner: Boss
prepared_by: Zero

# ============================================================
# 0. PURPOSE
# ============================================================

This document fixes the physical DDL direction for the
Public Company Intelligence domain.

The goal is to make later SQL creation stable by fixing:
- schema naming
- table naming
- primary key direction
- foreign key direction
- unique key direction
- index direction
- operational columns

# ============================================================
# 1. SCHEMA
# ============================================================

recommended_schema:
- business

reason:
- all applications are Persona-side
- this domain is a BusinessOS common foundation
- Persona-side DB already has an existing business schema
- business is more natural than ERP-only placement
- no new schema is required at this stage

# ============================================================
# 2. TABLE LIST
# ============================================================

tables:
- business.public_source_registry
- business.company_public_source_snapshot
- business.officer_public_source_snapshot
- business.company_public_profile
- business.company_officer_profile
- business.company_public_profile_source_link
- business.officer_profile_source_link
- business.company_normalization_candidate
- business.officer_normalization_candidate
- business.public_data_review_queue
- business.company_batch_job
- business.company_batch_job_log
- business.public_data_change_audit

# ============================================================
# 3. PRIMARY KEY DIRECTION
# ============================================================

primary_key_direction:
- every table has a single id primary key
- id type should follow existing Persona-side business schema convention
- created_at and updated_at should exist wherever lifecycle matters
- review / audit tables should preserve created_at at minimum

# ============================================================
# 4. FOREIGN KEY DIRECTION
# ============================================================

foreign_key_direction:

public_source_registry:
- no parent foreign key

company_public_source_snapshot:
- source_registry_id -> business.public_source_registry.public_source_registry_id

officer_public_source_snapshot:
- source_registry_id -> business.public_source_registry.public_source_registry_id

company_public_profile:
- no mandatory parent foreign key

company_officer_profile:
- company_public_profile_id -> business.company_public_profile.company_public_profile_id

company_public_profile_source_link:
- company_public_profile_id -> business.company_public_profile.company_public_profile_id
- source_snapshot_id -> business.company_public_source_snapshot.company_public_source_snapshot_id

officer_profile_source_link:
- company_officer_profile_id -> business.company_officer_profile.company_officer_profile_id
- source_snapshot_id -> business.officer_public_source_snapshot.officer_public_source_snapshot_id

company_normalization_candidate:
- candidate_company_public_profile_id -> business.company_public_profile.company_public_profile_id

officer_normalization_candidate:
- candidate_company_officer_profile_id -> business.company_officer_profile.company_officer_profile_id

public_data_review_queue:
- no mandatory parent foreign key because target_table / target_id is polymorphic

company_batch_job:
- no parent foreign key

company_batch_job_log:
- company_batch_job_id -> business.company_batch_job.company_batch_job_id
- source_registry_id -> business.public_source_registry.public_source_registry_id nullable

public_data_change_audit:
- batch_job_id -> business.company_batch_job.company_batch_job_id nullable

# ============================================================
# 5. UNIQUE KEY DIRECTION
# ============================================================

recommended_unique_keys:

public_source_registry:
- uq_public_source_registry_source_code (source_code)

company_public_source_snapshot:
- uq_company_public_source_snapshot_source_reference_hash
  (source_registry_id, source_reference, content_hash)

officer_public_source_snapshot:
- uq_officer_public_source_snapshot_source_reference_hash
  (source_registry_id, source_reference, content_hash)

company_public_profile:
- uq_company_public_profile_normalized_company_key (normalized_company_key)
- uq_company_public_profile_corporate_number (corporate_number) where corporate_number is not null

company_officer_profile:
- uq_company_officer_profile_company_officer_key
  (company_public_profile_id, normalized_officer_key)

company_public_profile_source_link:
- uq_company_profile_source_link_selected_field
  (company_public_profile_id, source_snapshot_id, field_name)

officer_profile_source_link:
- uq_officer_profile_source_link_selected_field
  (company_officer_profile_id, source_snapshot_id, field_name)

company_normalization_candidate:
- uq_company_normalization_candidate_identity
  (raw_company_name, normalized_company_key, candidate_company_public_profile_id)

officer_normalization_candidate:
- uq_officer_normalization_candidate_identity
  (raw_officer_name, raw_title, candidate_company_officer_profile_id)

# ============================================================
# 6. INDEX DIRECTION
# ============================================================

recommended_indexes:
- source enabled/source_type indexes
- snapshot source/fetched_at/hash support indexes
- company profile company_name/corporate_number/website/freshness indexes
- officer profile company/name/representative/review indexes
- candidate raw_name/review_status/match_score indexes
- review_queue status/issue_type/confidence/created_at indexes
- batch_job status/type/chunk_key/created_at indexes
- batch_job_log job/source/created_at/target indexes
- change_audit target/changed_at/batch_job indexes

# ============================================================
# 7. SUMMARY
# ============================================================

The physical backbone stays in the existing Persona-side
business schema because this is a BusinessOS common foundation
consumed by Persona-side applications.

# ============================================================

This document fixes the exact table contract before physical SQL generation.

It fixes:
- table names
- column names
- nullability direction
- default direction
- key columns
- state columns
- audit columns

# ============================================================
# 1. SCHEMA
# ============================================================

schema:
- business

# ============================================================
# 2. TABLES
# ============================================================

tables:
- business.public_source_registry
- business.company_public_source_snapshot
- business.officer_public_source_snapshot

- business.officer_profile_source_link

- business.officer_normalization_candidate
- business.public_data_review_queue

- business.company_batch_job_log

# ============================================================

# ============================================================

- parse_state
- parse_error_reason
- created_at

officer_public_source_snapshot_core_columns:
- officer_public_source_snapshot_id
- source_registry_id
- source_reference
- source_url
- fetched_at
- raw_company_name
- raw_officer_name
- raw_title
- raw_section_name
- raw_payload_json
- content_hash
- parse_state
- parse_error_reason
- created_at

- company_public_profile_id

- company_officer_profile_id

- representative_flag

- normalization_state
- review_required
- created_at

- chunk_key
- source_scope

- attempt_count
- success_count
- failure_count
- warning_count
- triggered_by
- created_at

# ============================================================
# 4. COMMON COLUMN RULES
# ============================================================

common_column_rules:
- created_at exists on every table
- updated_at exists where entity lifecycle matters
- raw_* columns preserve source expression
- normalized_* columns preserve derived output
- review_status defaults to pending where review workflow exists
- confidence_level defaults to unknown where confidence semantics exist
- review_required defaults to false and is raised explicitly
- job counters default to 0

# ============================================================
# 5. DIRECTION
# ============================================================

direction:
- exact SQL generation should now target business schema
- no ERP-only schema assumption remains
- this contract follows Persona-side application ownership

# ============================================================
# 6. SUMMARY
# ============================================================

This exact contract fixes the implementation-facing shape of
the Public Company Intelligence tables under the existing
business schema.

# ============================================================
# PUBLIC COMPANY INTELLIGENCE
# BUSINESS SCHEMA DDL DRAFT
# ============================================================

status: draft
system: business-os
domain: public-company-intelligence
db_position: persona-db / business schema
layer: 120.implementation
owner: Boss
prepared_by: Zero
note:
- design draft only
- not executed
- additive only
- target schema is existing business schema

# ============================================================
# 0. PURPOSE
# ============================================================

This document records the SQL-ready DDL draft direction for
Public Company Intelligence under the existing business schema.

This is not an execution artifact yet.
It is a design-fix artifact so later SQL generation can be
performed with lower ambiguity.

# ============================================================
# 1. TARGET OBJECTS
# ============================================================

target_tables:
- business.public_source_registry
- business.company_public_source_snapshot
- business.officer_public_source_snapshot
- business.company_public_profile
- business.company_officer_profile
- business.company_public_profile_source_link
- business.officer_profile_source_link
- business.company_normalization_candidate
- business.officer_normalization_candidate
- business.public_data_review_queue
- business.company_batch_job
- business.company_batch_job_log
- business.public_data_change_audit

target_views:
- business.v_pci_company_public_profile_latest
- business.v_pci_company_officer_profile_latest
- business.v_pci_company_grouping_support
- business.v_pci_publication_preflight_support
- business.v_pci_review_queue_open
- business.v_pci_batch_job_status_latest

# ============================================================
# 2. KEY NAMING DIRECTION
# ============================================================

primary_key_direction:
- single id primary key per table
- preserve existing business-schema style where possible
- ids should follow Persona-side business schema convention at SQL phase

foreign_key_direction:
- source_registry_id links to business.public_source_registry
- company_public_profile_id links company-officer and company-source-link tables
- company_officer_profile_id links officer-source-link tables
- batch_job_id links audit tables
- target_table + target_id remains polymorphic in review queue

# ============================================================
# 3. SQL DRAFT SHAPE
# ============================================================

sql_draft_shape:
- CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS business.public_source_registry (...)
- CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS business.company_public_source_snapshot (...)
- CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS business.officer_public_source_snapshot (...)
- CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS business.company_public_profile (...)
- CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS business.company_officer_profile (...)
- CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS business.company_public_profile_source_link (...)
- CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS business.officer_profile_source_link (...)
- CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS business.company_normalization_candidate (...)
- CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS business.officer_normalization_candidate (...)
- CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS business.public_data_review_queue (...)
- CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS business.company_batch_job (...)
- CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS business.company_batch_job_log (...)
- CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS business.public_data_change_audit (...)

# ============================================================
# 4. INDEX DIRECTION
# ============================================================

index_direction:
- source enable/type indexes
- snapshot source/fetched_at/parse_state indexes
- profile company-name/corporate-number/website/freshness indexes
- officer company/name/representative/review indexes
- candidate raw-name/review-status/match-score indexes
- review queue status/issue/confidence/created indexes
- batch job status/type/chunk indexes
- batch job log job/source/target indexes
- change audit target/changed_at/batch_job indexes

# ============================================================
# 5. UNIQUE DIRECTION
# ============================================================

unique_direction:
- public_source_registry.source_code unique
- company_public_profile.normalized_company_key unique
- company_public_profile.corporate_number partial unique when not null
- company_officer_profile (company_public_profile_id, normalized_officer_key) unique
- snapshot source_reference + content_hash uniqueness
- source-link field-level uniqueness by profile/snapshot/field

# ============================================================
# 6. VIEW DRAFT DIRECTION
# ============================================================

view_draft_direction:
- v_pci_company_public_profile_latest selects latest reusable public profile
- v_pci_company_officer_profile_latest selects latest reusable officer profile
- v_pci_company_grouping_support optimizes same-company lookup
- v_pci_publication_preflight_support optimizes preflight read
- v_pci_review_queue_open exposes pending review queue
- v_pci_batch_job_status_latest exposes latest job status read model

# ============================================================
# 7. COLUMN FAMILY DIRECTION
# ============================================================

column_family_direction:
- raw_* columns preserve source text
- normalized_* columns preserve derived values
- confidence_level and review_required remain explicit
- created_at on all tables
- updated_at on mutable lifecycle tables
- fetched_at on source snapshot tables
- latest_public_update_at and freshness_score on company profile
- review_status on candidate and review queue tables
- attempt_count/success_count/failure_count/warning_count on batch job

# ============================================================
# 8. NON-EXECUTION RULE
# ============================================================

non_execution_rule:
- this document fixes DDL direction only
- no SQL execution is performed at this stage
- actual SQL generation must be reviewed after existing business-schema style confirmation

# ============================================================
# 9. SUMMARY
# ============================================================

Public Company Intelligence should now be treated as:
- Persona-side
- BusinessOS common foundation
- stored in existing business schema
- still design-only
- ready for later SQL generation

# FILE: /data/data/com.termux/files/home/01.civilization-system/03.business-os/120.implementation/250.public-company-intelligence/1202514_PUBLIC_COMPANY_INTELLIGENCE_BUSINESS_SCHEMA_STYLE_ALIGNMENT.md
# ------------------------------------------------------------

# ============================================================
# PUBLIC COMPANY INTELLIGENCE
# BUSINESS SCHEMA STYLE ALIGNMENT
# ============================================================

status: draft
system: business-os
domain: public-company-intelligence
db_position: persona-db / business schema
layer: 120.implementation
owner: Boss
prepared_by: Zero
note:
- design-only
- style alignment against existing persona-side business schema
- additive only

# ============================================================
# 0. PURPOSE
# ============================================================

This document fixes the naming and column-style alignment for
Public Company Intelligence so it fits the existing
Persona-side business schema more naturally.

The goal is to reduce future mismatch in:
- table naming
- primary key naming
- foreign key naming
- timestamp naming
- status naming
- jsonb usage
- boolean usage

# ============================================================
# 1. EXISTING BUSINESS-SCHEMA STYLE IMPRESSION
# ============================================================

observed_style_impression:
- uuid usage is common
- created_at is broadly used
- updated_at exists only where lifecycle mutation matters
- status-like columns are common
- boolean flags are common
- jsonb is acceptable and normal
- some tables use generic id
- some tables use domain-specific *_id
- not every table follows one single rigid convention

# ============================================================
# 2. ALIGNMENT DECISION
# ============================================================

alignment_decision:
- keep table names domain-explicit
- keep primary keys domain-explicit rather than generic id
- keep foreign keys domain-explicit
- use created_at everywhere
- use updated_at only on mutable lifecycle tables
- use review_status / job_status / fetch_status as explicit domain statuses
- use jsonb for raw payload and flexible metadata
- use boolean flags only where semantics are truly boolean

reason:
- existing business schema tolerates mixed styles
- this domain is large enough that explicit ids improve readability
- future cross-table joins will be clearer with domain-explicit key names

# ============================================================
# 3. TABLE NAMING ALIGNMENT
# ============================================================

recommended_table_names:
- business.public_source_registry
- business.company_public_source_snapshot
- business.officer_public_source_snapshot
- business.company_public_profile
- business.company_officer_profile
- business.company_public_profile_source_link
- business.officer_profile_source_link
- business.company_normalization_candidate
- business.officer_normalization_candidate
- business.public_data_review_queue
- business.company_batch_job
- business.company_batch_job_log
- business.public_data_change_audit

table_naming_rule:
- use explicit business-domain nouns
- avoid over-short names
- avoid app-specific prefixes
- keep company / officer / public / review / batch semantics visible in the name

# ============================================================
# 4. PRIMARY KEY NAMING ALIGNMENT
# ============================================================

recommended_primary_key_names:
- public_source_registry_id
- company_public_source_snapshot_id
- officer_public_source_snapshot_id
- company_public_profile_id
- company_officer_profile_id
- company_public_profile_source_link_id
- officer_profile_source_link_id
- company_normalization_candidate_id
- officer_normalization_candidate_id
- public_data_review_queue_id
- company_batch_job_id
- company_batch_job_log_id
- public_data_change_audit_id

primary_key_rule:
- do not collapse everything to plain id
- use domain-explicit primary key names
- follow one explicit naming rule consistently inside this domain

reason:
- clearer SQL joins
- clearer review and audit references
- safer future code generation

# ============================================================
# 5. FOREIGN KEY NAMING ALIGNMENT
# ============================================================

recommended_foreign_key_names:
- source_registry_id
- company_public_profile_id
- company_officer_profile_id
- source_snapshot_id
- candidate_company_public_profile_id
- candidate_company_officer_profile_id
- batch_job_id

foreign_key_rule:
- foreign key names should reuse target primary-key meaning
- avoid ambiguous generic names like parent_id
- keep candidate_* naming where the relation is only a candidate

# ============================================================
# 6. TIMESTAMP COLUMN ALIGNMENT
# ============================================================

required_timestamp_columns_by_category:

all_tables:
- created_at

mutable_lifecycle_tables:
- updated_at

source_snapshot_tables:
- fetched_at
- source_published_at when available

profile_tables:
- latest_public_update_at

review_tables:
- reviewed_at when review outcome exists

batch_tables:
- scheduled_at
- started_at
- finished_at

timestamp_rule:
- created_at everywhere
- updated_at only where row mutation is meaningful
- keep fetched_at distinct from source_published_at
- keep batch lifecycle timestamps explicit

# ============================================================
# 7. STATUS COLUMN ALIGNMENT
# ============================================================

recommended_status_columns:
- robots_policy_status
- fetch_status
- parse_state
- normalization_state
- confidence_level
- review_status
- job_status
- company_status
- listed_status

status_rule:
- keep domain-specific status names
- do not overload one generic status column across all semantics
- use explicit review_status for review workflow
- use explicit job_status for batch execution
- use explicit fetch_status for source retrieval

# ============================================================
# 8. BOOLEAN COLUMN ALIGNMENT
# ============================================================

recommended_boolean_columns:
- attribution_required
- enabled
- representative_flag
- selected_for_profile
- review_required

boolean_rule:
- use boolean only for real binary semantics
- avoid replacing expressive statuses with booleans
- review_required stays boolean because it is a gate signal, not a lifecycle state

# ============================================================
# 9. JSONB ALIGNMENT
# ============================================================

recommended_jsonb_usage:
- raw_payload_json for source snapshots

optional_future_jsonb_usage:
- source_metadata_json
- matching_detail_json
- review_context_json

jsonb_rule:
- jsonb is acceptable for raw or flexible evidence structures
- normalized reusable profile fields should stay first-class columns
- do not hide important searchable fields inside jsonb only

# ============================================================
# 10. TEXT / NUMERIC ALIGNMENT
# ============================================================

recommended_core_scalar_types:
- names / urls / codes / summaries: text
- scores: numeric
- counts: integer
- flags: boolean
- times: timestamptz

scalar_rule:
- keep searchable identity fields as text columns
- keep match_score numeric
- keep freshness_score integer unless future scoring needs decimal precision

# ============================================================
# 11. UPDATED TABLE-BY-TABLE STYLE NOTE
# ============================================================

public_source_registry:
- keep updated_at
- source governance changes over time

company_public_source_snapshot:
- no updated_at required
- snapshot rows should be append-style

officer_public_source_snapshot:
- no updated_at required
- snapshot rows should be append-style

company_public_profile:
- keep updated_at
- profile is mutable and refreshed over time

company_officer_profile:
- keep updated_at
- officer profile is mutable and refreshed over time

company_public_profile_source_link:
- no updated_at required
- append-oriented evidence link is enough

officer_profile_source_link:
- no updated_at required
- append-oriented evidence link is enough

company_normalization_candidate:
- no updated_at required if review lifecycle is represented by reviewed_at and immutable candidate row policy
- updated_at may be added later only if mutation-heavy workflow is chosen

officer_normalization_candidate:
- same policy as company_normalization_candidate

public_data_review_queue:
- keep updated_at
- queue state changes over time

company_batch_job:
- no updated_at required
- lifecycle timestamps already exist

company_batch_job_log:
- no updated_at required
- append log only

public_data_change_audit:
- no updated_at required
- append audit only

# ============================================================
# 12. FINAL ALIGNMENT DECISION
# ============================================================

final_alignment_decision:
- use business schema
- use domain-explicit table names
- use domain-explicit primary keys
- use created_at broadly
- use updated_at selectively
- use explicit status columns by concern
- use jsonb only for raw / flexible payload areas
- preserve append-oriented design for snapshots, logs, and audits

# ============================================================
# 13. SUMMARY
# ============================================================

Public Company Intelligence should align to the Persona-side
business schema by matching its operational style, but it should
still keep explicit domain naming because this domain is large,
cross-cutting, and review-heavy.

That means:
- business schema: yes
- generic id everywhere: no
- domain-explicit ids: yes
- append-oriented evidence/log/audit tables: yes
- selective updated_at: yes

# ============================================================
# PUBLIC COMPANY INTELLIGENCE
# TABLE EXACT CONTRACT
# STYLE-ALIGNED V2
# ============================================================

status: draft
system: business-os
domain: public-company-intelligence
db_position: persona-db / business schema
layer: 120.implementation
owner: Boss
prepared_by: Zero
note:
- design-only
- not executed
- aligned to existing persona-side business schema style

# ============================================================
# 0. PURPOSE
# ============================================================

This document fixes the exact table contract after style alignment.

It reflects:
- business schema placement
- domain-explicit primary key naming
- selective updated_at usage
- append-oriented snapshot/log/audit design
- explicit status columns
- jsonb only where flexible raw payload is natural

# ============================================================
# 1. SCHEMA
# ============================================================

schema:
- business

# ============================================================
# 2. business.public_source_registry
# ============================================================

primary_key:
- public_source_registry_id

columns:
- public_source_registry_id:
    type: uuid
    null: false
- source_code:
    type: text
    null: false
- source_name:
    type: text
    null: false
- source_type:
    type: text
    null: false
- base_domain:
    type: text
    null: true
- access_method:
    type: text
    null: false
- robots_policy_status:
    type: text
    null: false
    default: unknown

# ============================================================
# 15. FINAL DIRECTION
# ============================================================

final_direction:
- business schema fixed
- uuid primary keys assumed for this domain
- domain-explicit primary key names retained
- append-oriented tables avoid updated_at
- mutable lifecycle tables keep updated_at
- raw payload uses jsonb
- explicit status columns remain separated by concern

# ============================================================
# 16. SUMMARY
# ============================================================

This style-aligned contract is the strongest pre-SQL version so far.

It is now aligned to:
- Persona-side ownership
- business schema placement
- existing business-schema style tolerance
- explicit domain readability
- append-oriented evidence and audit design

# ============================================================
# PUBLIC COMPANY INTELLIGENCE
# SQL DRAFT
# BUSINESS SCHEMA
# NON-EXECUTION
# ============================================================

status: draft
system: business-os
domain: public-company-intelligence
db_position: persona-db / business schema
layer: 120.implementation
owner: Boss
prepared_by: Zero
note:
- design-only
- not executed
- additive only
- aligned to persona-side business schema style

# ============================================================
# 0. PURPOSE
# ============================================================

This document stores the SQL draft body for later execution work.

It is intentionally design-only.
It exists so that:
- table creation direction is fixed
- column and constraint direction is visible
- future SQL execution can be reviewed before use

# ============================================================
# 1. SQL DRAFT BODY
# ============================================================

~~~sql
BEGIN;

-- ============================================================
-- 1. business.public_source_registry
-- ============================================================

CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS business.public_source_registry (
  public_source_registry_id uuid PRIMARY KEY,
  source_code text NOT NULL,
  source_name text NOT NULL,
  source_type text NOT NULL,
  base_domain text,
  access_method text NOT NULL,
  robots_policy_status text NOT NULL DEFAULT 'unknown',
  terms_checked_at timestamptz,
  rate_limit_rule text,
  attribution_required boolean NOT NULL DEFAULT false,
  enabled boolean NOT NULL DEFAULT true,
  disabled_reason text,
  owner_note text,
  created_at timestamptz NOT NULL DEFAULT now(),
  updated_at timestamptz NOT NULL DEFAULT now(),
  CONSTRAINT uq_public_source_registry_source_code UNIQUE (source_code)
);

-- ============================================================
-- 2. business.company_public_source_snapshot
-- ============================================================

CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS business.company_public_source_snapshot (
  company_public_source_snapshot_id uuid PRIMARY KEY,
  source_registry_id uuid NOT NULL,
  source_reference text NOT NULL,
  source_url text,
  source_document_type text NOT NULL,
  source_published_at timestamptz,
  fetched_at timestamptz NOT NULL,
  fetch_status text NOT NULL,
  http_status integer,
  raw_title text,
  raw_body text,
  raw_payload_json jsonb,
  content_hash text NOT NULL,
  detected_company_name text,
  detected_corporate_number text,
  detected_security_code text,
  parse_state text NOT NULL DEFAULT 'raw_only',
  parse_error_reason text,
  created_at timestamptz NOT NULL DEFAULT now(),
  CONSTRAINT fk_company_public_source_snapshot_source_registry
    FOREIGN KEY (source_registry_id)
    REFERENCES business.public_source_registry(public_source_registry_id),
  CONSTRAINT uq_company_public_source_snapshot_source_reference_hash
    UNIQUE (source_registry_id, source_reference, content_hash)
);

-- ============================================================
-- 3. business.officer_public_source_snapshot
-- ============================================================

CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS business.officer_public_source_snapshot (
  officer_public_source_snapshot_id uuid PRIMARY KEY,
  source_registry_id uuid NOT NULL,
  source_reference text NOT NULL,
  source_url text,
  fetched_at timestamptz NOT NULL,
  raw_company_name text,
  raw_officer_name text NOT NULL,
  raw_title text,
  raw_section_name text,
  raw_payload_json jsonb,
  content_hash text NOT NULL,
  parse_state text NOT NULL DEFAULT 'raw_only',
  parse_error_reason text,
  created_at timestamptz NOT NULL DEFAULT now(),
  CONSTRAINT fk_officer_public_source_snapshot_source_registry
    FOREIGN KEY (source_registry_id)
    REFERENCES business.public_source_registry(public_source_registry_id),
  CONSTRAINT uq_officer_public_source_snapshot_source_reference_hash
    UNIQUE (source_registry_id, source_reference, content_hash)
);

-- ============================================================
-- 4. business.company_public_profile
-- ============================================================

CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS business.company_public_profile (
  company_public_profile_id uuid PRIMARY KEY,
  normalized_company_key text NOT NULL,
  canonical_company_name text NOT NULL,
  company_name_kana text,
  corporate_number text,
  security_code text,
  website_url text,
  ir_url text,
  phone_number text,
  postal_address text,
  prefecture text,
  country_code text,
  industry_primary text,
  industry_secondary text,
  listed_status text NOT NULL DEFAULT 'unknown',
  market_name text,
  company_status text NOT NULL DEFAULT 'unknown',
  business_summary text,
  representative_name text,
  latest_public_update_at timestamptz,
  freshness_score integer NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
  normalization_state text NOT NULL DEFAULT 'raw_only',
  confidence_level text NOT NULL DEFAULT 'unknown',
  review_required boolean NOT NULL DEFAULT false,
  visibility_scope text NOT NULL DEFAULT 'public',
  created_at timestamptz NOT NULL DEFAULT now(),
  updated_at timestamptz NOT NULL DEFAULT now(),
  CONSTRAINT uq_company_public_profile_normalized_company_key
    UNIQUE (normalized_company_key)
);

-- ============================================================
-- 5. business.company_officer_profile
-- ============================================================

CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS business.company_officer_profile (
  company_officer_profile_id uuid PRIMARY KEY,
  company_public_profile_id uuid NOT NULL,
  normalized_officer_key text NOT NULL,
  canonical_officer_name text NOT NULL,
  canonical_title text,
  title_rank integer,
  officer_role_type text,
  representative_flag boolean NOT NULL DEFAULT false,
  source_count integer NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
  latest_source_at timestamptz,
  confidence_level text NOT NULL DEFAULT 'unknown',
  normalization_state text NOT NULL DEFAULT 'raw_only',
  review_required boolean NOT NULL DEFAULT false,
  created_at timestamptz NOT NULL DEFAULT now(),
  updated_at timestamptz NOT NULL DEFAULT now(),
  CONSTRAINT fk_company_officer_profile_company_public_profile
    FOREIGN KEY (company_public_profile_id)
    REFERENCES business.company_public_profile(company_public_profile_id),
  CONSTRAINT uq_company_officer_profile_company_officer_key
    UNIQUE (company_public_profile_id, normalized_officer_key)
);

-- ============================================================
-- 6. business.company_public_profile_source_link
-- ============================================================

CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS business.company_public_profile_source_link (
  company_public_profile_source_link_id uuid PRIMARY KEY,
  company_public_profile_id uuid NOT NULL,
  source_snapshot_id uuid NOT NULL,
  source_priority integer,
  field_name text NOT NULL,
  raw_value text,
  normalized_value text,
  selected_for_profile boolean NOT NULL DEFAULT false,
  confidence_level text NOT NULL DEFAULT 'unknown',
  created_at timestamptz NOT NULL DEFAULT now(),
  CONSTRAINT fk_company_public_profile_source_link_profile
    FOREIGN KEY (company_public_profile_id)
    REFERENCES business.company_public_profile(company_public_profile_id),
  CONSTRAINT fk_company_public_profile_source_link_snapshot
    FOREIGN KEY (source_snapshot_id)
    REFERENCES business.company_public_source_snapshot(company_public_source_snapshot_id),
  CONSTRAINT uq_company_public_profile_source_link_field
    UNIQUE (company_public_profile_id, source_snapshot_id, field_name)
);

-- ============================================================
-- 7. business.officer_profile_source_link
-- ============================================================

CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS business.officer_profile_source_link (
  officer_profile_source_link_id uuid PRIMARY KEY,
  company_officer_profile_id uuid NOT NULL,
  source_snapshot_id uuid NOT NULL,
  source_priority integer,
  field_name text NOT NULL,
  raw_value text,
  normalized_value text,
  selected_for_profile boolean NOT NULL DEFAULT false,
  confidence_level text NOT NULL DEFAULT 'unknown',
  created_at timestamptz NOT NULL DEFAULT now(),
  CONSTRAINT fk_officer_profile_source_link_profile
    FOREIGN KEY (company_officer_profile_id)
    REFERENCES business.company_officer_profile(company_officer_profile_id),
  CONSTRAINT fk_officer_profile_source_link_snapshot
    FOREIGN KEY (source_snapshot_id)
    REFERENCES business.officer_public_source_snapshot(officer_public_source_snapshot_id),
  CONSTRAINT uq_officer_profile_source_link_field
    UNIQUE (company_officer_profile_id, source_snapshot_id, field_name)
);

-- ============================================================
-- 8. business.company_normalization_candidate
-- ============================================================

CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS business.company_normalization_candidate (
  company_normalization_candidate_id uuid PRIMARY KEY,
  raw_company_name text NOT NULL,
  normalized_company_key text NOT NULL,
  candidate_company_public_profile_id uuid,
  match_method text NOT NULL,
  match_score numeric,
  review_required boolean NOT NULL DEFAULT false,
  review_status text NOT NULL DEFAULT 'pending',
  reviewer_id text,
  reviewed_at timestamptz,
  created_at timestamptz NOT NULL DEFAULT now(),
  CONSTRAINT fk_company_normalization_candidate_profile
    FOREIGN KEY (candidate_company_public_profile_id)
    REFERENCES business.company_public_profile(company_public_profile_id),
  CONSTRAINT uq_company_normalization_candidate_identity
    UNIQUE (raw_company_name, normalized_company_key, candidate_company_public_profile_id)
);

-- ============================================================
-- 9. business.officer_normalization_candidate
-- ============================================================

CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS business.officer_normalization_candidate (
  officer_normalization_candidate_id uuid PRIMARY KEY,
  raw_officer_name text NOT NULL,
  raw_title text,
  candidate_company_officer_profile_id uuid,
  match_method text NOT NULL,
  match_score numeric,
  review_required boolean NOT NULL DEFAULT false,
  review_status text NOT NULL DEFAULT 'pending',
  reviewer_id text,
  reviewed_at timestamptz,
  created_at timestamptz NOT NULL DEFAULT now(),
  CONSTRAINT fk_officer_normalization_candidate_profile
    FOREIGN KEY (candidate_company_officer_profile_id)
    REFERENCES business.company_officer_profile(company_officer_profile_id),
  CONSTRAINT uq_officer_normalization_candidate_identity
    UNIQUE (raw_officer_name, raw_title, candidate_company_officer_profile_id)
);

-- ============================================================
-- 10. business.public_data_review_queue
-- ============================================================

CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS business.public_data_review_queue (
  public_data_review_queue_id uuid PRIMARY KEY,
  queue_type text NOT NULL,
  target_table text NOT NULL,
  target_id text NOT NULL,
  issue_type text NOT NULL,
  issue_summary text NOT NULL,
  confidence_level text NOT NULL DEFAULT 'unknown',
  suggested_action text,
  review_status text NOT NULL DEFAULT 'pending',
  created_at timestamptz NOT NULL DEFAULT now(),
  updated_at timestamptz NOT NULL DEFAULT now()
);

-- ============================================================
-- 11. business.company_batch_job
-- ============================================================

CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS business.company_batch_job (
  company_batch_job_id uuid PRIMARY KEY,
  job_type text NOT NULL,
  scheduled_at timestamptz,
  started_at timestamptz,
  finished_at timestamptz,
  job_status text NOT NULL,
  chunk_key text,
  source_scope text,
  target_scope text,
  attempt_count integer NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
  success_count integer NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
  failure_count integer NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
  warning_count integer NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
  triggered_by text NOT NULL DEFAULT 'system',
  created_at timestamptz NOT NULL DEFAULT now()
);

-- ============================================================
-- 12. business.company_batch_job_log
-- ============================================================

CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS business.company_batch_job_log (
  company_batch_job_log_id uuid PRIMARY KEY,
  company_batch_job_id uuid NOT NULL,
  log_level text NOT NULL,
  source_registry_id uuid,
  target_type text,
  target_id text,
  message_code text,
  message_text text NOT NULL,
  error_detail text,
  created_at timestamptz NOT NULL DEFAULT now(),
  CONSTRAINT fk_company_batch_job_log_job
    FOREIGN KEY (company_batch_job_id)
    REFERENCES business.company_batch_job(company_batch_job_id),
  CONSTRAINT fk_company_batch_job_log_source_registry
    FOREIGN KEY (source_registry_id)
    REFERENCES business.public_source_registry(public_source_registry_id)
);

-- ============================================================
-- 13. business.public_data_change_audit
-- ============================================================

CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS business.public_data_change_audit (
  public_data_change_audit_id uuid PRIMARY KEY,
  target_type text NOT NULL,
  target_id text NOT NULL,
  changed_field text NOT NULL,
  before_value text,
  after_value text,
  source_basis text,
  change_reason text,
  changed_at timestamptz NOT NULL,
  batch_job_id uuid,
  CONSTRAINT fk_public_data_change_audit_batch_job
    FOREIGN KEY (batch_job_id)
    REFERENCES business.company_batch_job(company_batch_job_id)
);

COMMIT;
~~~

BEGIN;

# ============================================================
# 2. VIEW SQL DRAFT
# ============================================================

~~~sql
BEGIN;

-- ============================================================
-- v_pci_company_public_profile_latest
-- ============================================================

CREATE OR REPLACE VIEW business.v_pci_company_public_profile_latest AS
SELECT
  p.company_public_profile_id,
  p.normalized_company_key,
  p.canonical_company_name,
  p.company_name_kana,
  p.corporate_number,
  p.security_code,
  p.website_url,
  p.ir_url,
  p.phone_number,
  p.postal_address,
  p.prefecture,
  p.country_code,
  p.industry_primary,
  p.industry_secondary,
  p.listed_status,
  p.market_name,
  p.company_status,
  p.business_summary,
  p.representative_name,
  p.latest_public_update_at,
  p.freshness_score,
  CASE
    WHEN p.latest_public_update_at IS NULL THEN 'unknown'
    WHEN p.latest_public_update_at < now() - interval '90 days' THEN 'stale'
    ELSE 'fresh'
  END AS freshness_state,
  p.confidence_level,
  p.review_required,
  p.updated_at
FROM business.company_public_profile p;

-- ============================================================
-- v_pci_company_officer_profile_latest
-- ============================================================

CREATE OR REPLACE VIEW business.v_pci_company_officer_profile_latest AS
SELECT
  o.company_officer_profile_id,
  o.company_public_profile_id,
  o.normalized_officer_key,
  o.canonical_officer_name,
  o.canonical_title,
  o.title_rank,
  o.officer_role_type,
  o.representative_flag,
  o.source_count,
  o.latest_source_at,
  o.confidence_level,
  o.review_required,
  o.updated_at
FROM business.company_officer_profile o;

-- ============================================================
-- v_pci_company_grouping_support
-- ============================================================

CREATE OR REPLACE VIEW business.v_pci_company_grouping_support AS
SELECT
  p.company_public_profile_id,
  p.canonical_company_name,
  p.normalized_company_key,
  p.corporate_number,
  p.website_url,
  p.phone_number,
  p.postal_address,
  p.listed_status,
  p.latest_public_update_at,
  p.freshness_score,
  CASE
    WHEN p.latest_public_update_at IS NULL THEN 'unknown'
    WHEN p.latest_public_update_at < now() - interval '90 days' THEN 'stale'
    ELSE 'fresh'
  END AS freshness_state,
  p.confidence_level,
  p.review_required
FROM business.company_public_profile p;

-- ============================================================
-- v_pci_publication_preflight_support
-- ============================================================

CREATE OR REPLACE VIEW business.v_pci_publication_preflight_support AS
SELECT
  p.company_public_profile_id,
  p.canonical_company_name,
  p.corporate_number,
  p.website_url,
  p.phone_number,
  p.postal_address,
  p.representative_name,
  p.latest_public_update_at,
  p.freshness_score,
  CASE
    WHEN p.latest_public_update_at IS NULL THEN 'unknown'
    WHEN p.latest_public_update_at < now() - interval '90 days' THEN 'stale'
    ELSE 'fresh'
  END AS freshness_state,
  p.confidence_level,
  p.review_required
FROM business.company_public_profile p;

-- ============================================================
-- v_pci_review_queue_open
-- ============================================================

CREATE OR REPLACE VIEW business.v_pci_review_queue_open AS
SELECT
  q.public_data_review_queue_id,
  q.queue_type,
  q.target_table,
  q.target_id,
  q.issue_type,
  q.issue_summary,
  q.confidence_level,
  q.suggested_action,
  q.review_status,
  q.created_at,
  q.updated_at
FROM business.public_data_review_queue q
WHERE q.review_status = 'pending';

-- ============================================================
-- v_pci_batch_job_status_latest
-- ============================================================

CREATE OR REPLACE VIEW business.v_pci_batch_job_status_latest AS
SELECT
  j.company_batch_job_id,
  j.job_type,
  j.scheduled_at,
  j.started_at,
  j.finished_at,
  j.job_status,
  j.chunk_key,
  j.source_scope,
  j.target_scope,
  j.attempt_count,
  j.success_count,
  j.failure_count,
  j.warning_count,
  j.created_at
FROM business.company_batch_job j;

COMMIT;
~~~

# FILE: /data/data/com.termux/files/home/01.civilization-system/03.business-os/130.development/1301491_BUSINESS_PERSONA_CONNECTION_IMPLEMENTATION_ROADMAP_FIXED.md
# ------------------------------------------------------------

# ============================================================
# BUSINESS PERSONA CONNECTION IMPLEMENTATION ROADMAP FIXED
# ============================================================

status: canonical
layer: development
system: business-os
owner: Boss
prepared_by: Zero

purpose:
Defines the fixed implementation roadmap
for BusinessOS -> PersonaOS connection,
using the uploaded Persona-side real DB as the first landing path.

# ============================================================
# 1. ROADMAP PRINCIPLE
# ============================================================

principle:
Prefer existing real Persona-side DB structures first.

principle:
Do not begin by adding new Persona-side tables
when growth_events and growth_core_state are already sufficient
for the first implementation-preparation path.

principle:
Fix transport, validation, idempotency, and apply path
before adding richer Persona-side relation models.

# ============================================================
# 2. FIXED PHASE ORDER
# ============================================================

fixed_phase_order:
- phase_1_effect_payload_and_auth
- phase_2_event_insert_path
- phase_3_growth_apply_path
- phase_4_duplicate_and_failure_hardening
- phase_5_optional_persona_table_extension

# ============================================================
# 3. PHASE 1 EFFECT PAYLOAD AND AUTH
# ============================================================

phase_name:
phase_1_effect_payload_and_auth

goal:
Fix exact payload and trusted-caller path.

must_complete:
- exact effect event payload fixed
- exact validation matrix fixed
- trusted BusinessOS caller rule fixed
- event_id idempotency rule fixed
- event_type and magnitude set fixed

exit_criteria:
- BusinessOS can form canonical payload
- PersonaOS can validate payload shape
- unauthorized caller is rejected
- invalid event_type is rejected
- invalid magnitude is rejected

# ============================================================
# 4. PHASE 2 EVENT INSERT PATH
# ============================================================

phase_name:
phase_2_event_insert_path

goal:
Land valid BusinessOS-origin events into personaos.growth_events.

must_complete:
- request endpoint
- payload validation
- growth_events insert mapping
- received_at population
- is_processed initial false
- processed_at initial null

target_table:
- personaos.growth_events

exit_criteria:
- valid event stored in growth_events
- duplicate event_id does not reinsert
- rejected payload does not reach storage

# ============================================================
# 5. PHASE 3 GROWTH APPLY PATH
# ============================================================

phase_name:
phase_3_growth_apply_path

goal:
Apply accepted events into personaos.growth_core_state.

must_complete:
- unprocessed event reader
- event_type to state-apply mapping
- trust apply
- familiarity apply
- relationship_score apply
- last_interaction_at update
- is_processed true update
- processed_at update

target_table:
- personaos.growth_core_state

exit_criteria:
- accepted event updates growth_core_state
- processed flag is updated
- same event does not apply twice

# ============================================================
# 6. PHASE 4 DUPLICATE AND FAILURE HARDENING
# ============================================================

phase_name:
phase_4_duplicate_and_failure_hardening

goal:
Make connection path reliable and safe.

must_complete:
- duplicate_ignored behavior
- processing_failed behavior
- retry or investigation strategy
- audit visibility
- invalid payload rejection logging
- invalid_effect_source handling

exit_criteria:
- duplicate event_id safely ignored
- apply failures are visible
- rejected events are explainable
- no silent double-apply occurs

# ============================================================
# 7. PHASE 5 OPTIONAL PERSONA TABLE EXTENSION
# ============================================================

phase_name:
phase_5_optional_persona_table_extension

goal:
Add richer Persona-side structures only if existing tables become insufficient.

later_candidates:
- persona_company_relation_state
- persona_reliability_perception
- business_effect_receipt
- business_effect_apply_audit

rule:
This phase is optional
and must not block the first implementation path.

exit_criteria:
- only start if real gaps are proven
- not started merely because richer design exists on paper

# ============================================================
# 8. FIXED BUILD ORDER INSIDE EACH PHASE
# ============================================================

build_order_inside_phase:
1. payload/interface
2. validation
3. storage mapping
4. apply logic
5. duplicate/idempotency logic
6. audit/monitoring hooks

rule:
Do not begin with UI.
Do not begin with new Persona-side tables.

# ============================================================
# 9. FIXED TEST GATES
# ============================================================

gate_1_payload:
- valid payload accepted
- invalid payload rejected
- unauthorized caller rejected

gate_2_insert:
- growth_events insert succeeds
- duplicate event_id ignored
- required context keys validated

gate_3_apply:
- trust updated
- familiarity updated
- relationship_score updated
- last_interaction_at updated
- processed flags updated

gate_4_hardening:
- duplicate safe
- processing failure visible
- invalid source visible

# ============================================================
# 10. STOP CONDITIONS
# ============================================================

must_stop_and_fix_before_next_phase_when:
- event_id idempotency is not guaranteed
- BusinessOS payload diverges from fixed contract
- Persona insert mapping diverges from growth_events real columns
- growth_core_state apply writes to wrong fields
- duplicate event causes double state mutation
- unauthorized caller can insert events

# ============================================================
# 11. OFFICIAL SUMMARY
# ============================================================

The fixed implementation order for BusinessOS -> PersonaOS connection is:

1. exact payload and authorization
2. growth_events insert path
3. growth_core_state apply path
4. duplicate and failure hardening
5. optional Persona-side richer tables only if needed

This roadmap is intentionally real-DB-first
and avoids premature new schema expansion.



# ------------------------------------------------------------

# ------------------------------------------------------------
# FILE: /data/data/com.termux/files/home/01.civilization-system/03.business-os/130.development/140.business-ai-worker/1301430_BUSINESS_AI_WORKER_IMPLEMENTATION_ROADMAP_FIXED.md
# ------------------------------------------------------------

# ============================================================
# BUSINESS AI WORKER IMPLEMENTATION ROADMAP FIXED
# ============================================================

status: canonical
layer: development
domain: business-ai-worker
system: business-os
owner: Boss
prepared_by: Zero

purpose:
Defines the fixed implementation roadmap
for Business AI Worker.

# ============================================================
# 1. ROADMAP PRINCIPLE
# ============================================================

principle:
Build control first,
then capacity,
then protected advisory,
then execution work,
then embedded app usage,
then hardening.

reason:
If UI or app-side work starts before foundation control,
lending truth, reservation truth, disclaimer truth,
and approval boundaries will fragment.

# ============================================================
# 2. FIXED PHASE ORDER
# ============================================================

fixed_phase_order:
- phase_1_foundation_control
- phase_2_capacity_and_matching
- phase_3_protected_advisory
- phase_4_execution_work
- phase_5_embedded_app_surfaces
- phase_6_monitoring_audit_hardening

# ============================================================
# 3. PHASE 1 FOUNDATION CONTROL
# ============================================================

phase_name:
phase_1_foundation_control

goal:
Establish BusinessOS foundation web as the single worker control tower.

must_complete:
- worker registry
- rank registry
- subscription handling
- lending request endpoint
- release endpoint
- status query endpoint
- exact enums fixed
- exact payload fixed
- physical schema fixed

exit_criteria:
- lend request can return granted / queued / rejected
- release updates lending and slot state
- status query returns canonical state
- no consumer app owns lending truth

# ============================================================
# 4. PHASE 2 CAPACITY AND MATCHING
# ============================================================

phase_name:
phase_2_capacity_and_matching

goal:
Make governed capacity and compatible matching work correctly.

must_complete:
- slot capacity logic
- reservation queue
- queue promotion
- specialty registry
- knowledge-depth registry
- world-scope validation
- activity-mode validation
- capability-aware match engine

exit_criteria:
- free slot + compatible worker => granted
- no slot + compatible worker => queued
- incompatible worker => rejected
- queue promotion works after release

# ============================================================
# 5. PHASE 3 PROTECTED ADVISORY
# ============================================================

phase_name:
phase_3_protected_advisory

goal:
Support governed advisory sessions including protected domains.

must_complete:
- disclaimer fetch endpoint
- consent submit endpoint
- advisory start endpoint
- advisory session persistence
- protected domain mapping
- consent validity checks
- escalation linkage

protected_domains:
- medical
- legal
- high-risk management advice

exit_criteria:
- protected advisory cannot start without disclaimer and consent
- non-protected advisory can start without protected flow
- advisory sessions are auditable

# ============================================================
# 6. PHASE 4 EXECUTION WORK
# ============================================================

phase_name:
phase_4_execution_work

goal:
Support governed execution work flows.

must_complete:
- execution start endpoint
- execution task persistence
- output handoff endpoint
- review_required logic
- approval_required logic
- marketplace / maintenance / bugfix / testing path support

examples:
- marketplace listing
- yahoo auctions listing
- mercari listing
- night maintenance
- bug fix support
- testing support

exit_criteria:
- execution task can start and track status
- handoff can become handoff_ready
- review and approval gates block when required

# ============================================================
# 7. PHASE 5 EMBEDDED APP SURFACES
# ============================================================

phase_name:
phase_5_embedded_app_surfaces

goal:
Allow first-party business apps to consume governed worker capacity.

must_complete:
- embedded app request flow
- app-surface binding
- routine assistance linkage
- workflow-completion release logic

examples:
- PocketSecretary
- expense
- CRM
- project
- MBO

exit_criteria:
- embedded surfaces can request workers through foundation
- embedded surfaces do not duplicate worker control logic
- routine assistance releases correctly on completion

# ============================================================
# 8. PHASE 6 MONITORING AUDIT HARDENING
# ============================================================

phase_name:
phase_6_monitoring_audit_hardening

goal:
Make the platform operable and safe at scale.

must_complete:
- audit trace
- queue monitoring
- slot anomaly monitoring
- failed handoff monitoring
- protected advisory audit
- anti-bypass checks
- fairness review support
- runbook support

exit_criteria:
- end-to-end trace exists
- incidents are detectable
- protected-domain misuse is visible
- queue starvation is reviewable

# ============================================================
# 9. FIXED BUILD ORDER INSIDE PHASES
# ============================================================

build_order_inside_phase:
1. model
2. interface
3. implementation
4. runtime
5. flow verification
6. operations hooks
7. policy/security verification

rule:
Do not build UI-first for worker governance features.

# ============================================================
# 10. CONSUMER APP START TIMING
# ============================================================

advisory_apps_may_start_after:
- phase_3_protected_advisory

execution_work_apps_may_start_after:
- phase_4_execution_work

embedded_app_surfaces_may_start_after:
- phase_5_embedded_app_surfaces

rule:
Consumer apps may prototype earlier,
but must not claim canonical behavior
before the corresponding foundation phase exits.

# ============================================================
# 11. FIXED TEST GATES
# ============================================================

gate_1_foundation:
- payload exactness pass
- enum exactness pass
- lending/release/status pass

gate_2_capacity:
- reservation pass
- queue promotion pass
- specialty/depth/world matching pass

gate_3_advisory:
- disclaimer pass
- consent pass
- protected advisory blocking pass

gate_4_execution:
- execution task pass
- review/approval blocking pass
- output handoff pass

gate_5_consumer:
- embedded app consumption pass
- advisory app integration pass
- execution app integration pass

gate_6_hardening:
- audit pass
- monitoring pass
- anti-bypass pass

# ============================================================
# 12. STOP CONDITIONS
# ============================================================

must_stop_and_fix_before_next_phase_when:
- exact payload and DB mapping diverge
- enum values diverge between API and DB
- consumer app bypasses foundation
- protected advisory starts without consent
- execution output bypasses review/approval
- queue promotion breaks rank/capacity rules

# ============================================================
# 13. OFFICIAL SUMMARY
# ============================================================

The fixed implementation order is:

1. foundation control
2. capacity and matching
3. protected advisory
4. execution work
5. embedded app surfaces
6. monitoring, audit, and hardening

This order is mandatory
to preserve governance and avoid fragmented worker truth.
